### **POLISHED ICE: A LEGEND IS BORN**  

Jodi had barely sat down.  

She had barely even *processed* the glorious, sizzling steak in front of her, still hot from the grill. The first bite was inches from her lips. She was warm, full of beer but finally free of the **bladder crisis** that had nearly ended her life in the bar’s port-a-let nightmare.  

And then?  

The **entire goddamn room** exploded into howling laughter.  

Jodi blinked. A shadow flickered across the bar as the projector roared to life, casting an enormous image onto the wall. A chill ran up her spine. The laughter grew louder.  

She turned her head.  

And **there she was.**  

Her **own goddamn tits** were now *two stories tall.*  

Projected in glorious **high-resolution military photography,** captured from an **F-35 fighter jet** at the exact moment she had grabbed her chest mid-flight, squinting toward her Gulfstream in confused panic.  

Jodi froze.  

The room **lost its fucking mind.**  

Soldiers were barking. **Actual barking.** Tables rattled as fists slammed down in glee. Beer sloshed from mugs as men *doubled over laughing.* The bartender wiped away **tears** of pure joy. Someone dropped to their knees, hands in the air, like they had just witnessed **the Second Coming of Christ.**  

Løytnant Tandstad, perched calmly at the bar, smirked into her drink.  

Jodi inhaled. Exhaled. Tapped the table once.  

“…So. Just checking. How classified is this photo?”  

A nearby sergeant wheezed, **“It was classified.”**  

More howling laughter.  

Jodi took another deep breath. Then, slowly, she turned to Tandstad, eyes narrowing.  

“You let a *fighter jet* take a photo of me **cupping my own tits?**”  

Tandstad shrugged. **"I didn't *let* them. They just did."**  

Jodi smacked her forehead.  

The general—**the actual base general, a short king who could probably drink her under the table**—grinned and raised his beer.  

“**To Polished Ice!**”  

The entire goddamn room erupted:  

**“POLISHED ICE! POLISHED ICE! POLISHED ICE!”**  

Jodi, doomed beyond reason, grabbed her beer and **drank deep.**

---
### **JODI, NOW TWO STORIES TALL, FACES HER DESTINY**  

Jodi stared up at her **massive, military-grade tit projection.**  

Her **48DDD chest** loomed over the entire room, perfectly framed by cutting-edge **F-35 targeting optics.** The sharp contrast, the impeccable focus—honestly? It was a **fantastic** shot. If she hadn’t been the **goddamn subject,** she might’ve been impressed.  

But she was **absolutely hammered,** and her brain was struggling to process anything beyond *beer good, steak warm, tits…big?*  

Then came the next blow.  

Tandstad, sipping her drink like she hadn’t just ruined Jodi’s entire existence, casually leaned in and murmured:  

**“Norwegian Air Force social media has been blowing up all day. They want some official photos. Would that be okay?”**  

Jodi’s soul **left her body.**  

She turned slowly—deliberately—**drunk as fuck**—and just *stared* at Tandstad.  

The soldiers, still **losing their goddamn minds,** were barking and chanting her callsign, **“POLISHED ICE! POLISHED ICE!”** But Jodi barely heard them.  

Her brain latched onto one key fact.  

The **Norwegian Armed Forces**—**an actual, legitimate military institution**—**wanted to post official photos of her.**  

Like she was a **fucking influencer.**  

Like she was a **mascot.**  

Like she was their **drunken, tit-cupping patron saint of chaos.**  

Jodi exhaled, slow. Then blinked.  

**“Tandstad. Babe. Angel. Sweetheart. Tell me something.”**  

Tandstad raised an eyebrow.  

Jodi gestured vaguely at the **two-story tits.**  

**“Do I have veto power, or am I already fucked?”**  

Tandstad took a slow sip of her drink. Thought about it.  

Then, finally, she smirked.  

**“Oh, you’re already fucked.”**  

Jodi slumped forward onto the bar. **Fuck.**  

A friendly corporal patted her back, trying to console her.  

**“Hey, you don’t *have* to smile for the new pictures! But, uh… you *should.*”**  

Jodi lifted her head just enough to glare. **“…Why?”**  

The corporal grinned.  

**“Because you’re kind of the Norwegian military’s biggest meme right now.”**  

The room **exploded** with laughter again.  

Jodi, feeling herself **descend deeper into beer-soaked doom,** squeezed her eyes shut and muttered:  

**“…I’m gonna need another drink.”**

---

### **THE AUTOGRAPH GAUNTLET: POLISHED ICE ASCENDS**  

Jodi had signed **so many goddamn autographs** that she was starting to forget what her own name looked like.  

At some point, her beer had been **replaced** by another beer. Then another. And another. She hadn’t even asked—**the beers just kept appearing.** She was **starting to feel it,** moving through the motions on pure instinct, her hand scrawling *Jodi Anderson* (*Polished Ice* was added by the more persistent ones) over shirts, notebooks, tactical gear, and—once—**a bare ass cheek.**  

That guy got a **special flourish.**  

But what was **really fucking with her** was the **sheer number of men** who looked like they had been **forged in the mountains by Odin himself.**  

Norway hadn’t been kidding about their national aesthetic.  

**Beer. Metal. Beards.**  

That was **exactly** what she was getting.  

Everywhere she looked—**burly commandos in pullover sweaters, thick beards, and piercing eyes**. Half of them looked like they’d been yanked from a **Viking warband** and just *happened* to pick up a modern-day rifle along the way.  

And they were all **so fucking excited** to meet her.  

They slapped her on the back, barked her callsign, cheered every time she chugged her beer like **a true warrior of the North.**  

One guy—**a blonde, tattooed menace with shoulders like a goddamn grizzly bear**—grinned as she signed his forearm.  

**“Polished Ice,”** he rumbled, accent thick, **“You are one of us now.”**  

Another commando—**a beast of a man with a scar down his cheek and an absolutely ridiculous silver braid in his beard**—leaned over with a smirk.  

**“I have never seen a civilian survive an extraction like that without shitting themselves. If you ever want to quit your band, we have a place for you.”**  

Jodi, **several beers deep,** burst out laughing.  

**“Tempting. I’d *love* to know what the fuck my job would even be.”**  

Scar-Braid just grinned.  

**“Drinking. Fighting. Scaring Americans.”**  

Jodi **wheezed.** **Tandstad, the traitorous menace, simply nodded.**  

This was her life now.  

And the **worst fucking part?**  

She was **starting to enjoy it.**

### **VIKINGS WERE SCARY—BUT THE WOMEN? THEY WERE **FUCKING TERRIFYING**.**  

Jodi had spent the last two hours drowning in beer, metal, and **two hundred bearded commandos** who all looked like they could **punch out a polar bear and fuck its widow.**  

These guys were **huge.** Grinning, tattooed, dangerous. **Viking-core as hell.**  

But the **women?**  

**The women were worse.**  

Every time she locked eyes with one, a primal **survival instinct** told her: *don’t fuck with her.*  

They all had that **same** look—**lethal. Ice-cold. Built for war.**  

Blonde hair. Blue eyes. Small chests. Compact, deadly frames. They weren’t **delicate Nordic angels.** They were **wolves in human skin.**  

Jodi swore, *swore,* that the moment she made eye contact with one, the woman just *knew* every **weak point in her body.**  

She’d seen some **killer-looking** women in her life.  

These bitches?  

They weren’t **killer-looking.** They were just **killers.**  

One of them—**a terrifying five-foot-six menace with her blonde hair pulled into a brutal, efficient bun**—stalked past Jodi, barely sparing her a glance. But as she passed, she muttered in **flawless, ice-cold English**—  

**“You’ll get used to us.”**  

Jodi **fucking shivered.**  

Tandstad, ever the smug bastard, just **grinned** and raised her beer.  

“**Like I said.** You’re one of us now.”  

Jodi exhaled. *Jesus Christ on a stick.*  

The **men** looked like Vikings.  

The **women** were **actual, modern-day Valkyries.**  

And somehow?  

**She was drinking with all of them.**

Her **boobs were immortalized in laser-engraved glass.**  

The Norwegian **Armed Forces** had given her **a goddamn plaque** like she was some kind of **war hero.**  

And now?  

Now she had to **survive the flight back.**  

Løytnant Tandstad, sitting next to her at the bar, leaned in with that **same smug, vaguely amused expression** she’d had since the very beginning of this whole nightmare.

Jodi, **already suspicious**, squinted at her.  

**“…Why?”**  

Tandstad **grinned.**  

**“So we don’t fly into a mountain.”**  

Jodi **blinked.** Took a slow, deliberate sip of her beer. Then nodded.

Tandstad **actually looked impressed.**  

She gestured toward Jodi with her beer, nodding.  

**“That’s true. You didn’t puke. Or shit yourself. Outstanding.”**  

A soldier at the next table—a **monstrous six-foot-four beast of a man with a beard like a **Viking warlord**—**slammed his fist on the wood in agreement.**  

**“YES. AMERICAN STRONG.”**  

More soldiers **cheered.** Someone barked. Someone else slammed **another** beer in front of Jodi, just in case she wanted to celebrate this **great achievement.**

But as **fun** as the **beer, beards, and unhinged Viking chaos** had been, Jodi was **so ready to be done.**  

Then, finally—**a miracle.**  

Tandstad, casually scrolling through her phone, hummed thoughtfully before **leaning over.**  

**“By the way. Air Force has been in contact with your band’s manager.”**  

Jodi, mid-sip, **froze.**  

Slowly, she turned, eyes **wide with immediate suspicion.**  

**“…Why?”**  

Tandstad’s lips **curved into that familiar smirk.**  

**“They’re flying you straight back to your hotel.”**  

Jodi felt something that could only be described as **pure fucking relief.**  

She dropped her head **back against the bar**, exhaled **hard**, and muttered—  

**“Thank *God.*”**  

No driving. No stops. No *extra* rounds of Viking insanity.  

Just a **straight shot back to whatever the fuck normal life was supposed to be.**  

Tandstad chuckled, clearly **enjoying** Jodi’s suffering.  

**“Grateful, are we?”**  

Jodi waved a hand **vaguely.**  

**“Babe. Angel. I adore you. But I have had a *very long day* full of *very big tits*—most of them mine—and I just need to pass the fuck out before something else insane happens.”**  

Tandstad just **grinned.**  

She **definitely** knew something Jodi didn’t.  

But Jodi, **blessedly ignorant**, just **thanked whatever gods were listening** that she was finally **going home.**

Jeff, immediately concerned, **looked up.**  

**“Where the fuck is Jodi?”**  

Tara **hesitated.**  

Then she turned her phone around.  

The table **leaned in.**

### **THE LANDING: ONE LAST SHOW OF FORCE**

And then?

Like a **fucking action movie.**  

**Four soldiers immediately hit the ground.**  

**Full kit. Full beards. Full, terrifying intensity.**

**Jodi.**  

And **Tandstad.**  

Jodi **wasn’t doing great.**  

She was **damn cold**—the **Arctic wind** ripping straight through her—**but she was also damn drunk.**  

She moved **slowly, deliberately, like someone trying *very* hard to prove they weren’t wasted.**  

One step. Then another.  

Her **laser-etched boob plaque was tucked under one arm.**  

Her **other hand was locked around Tandstad’s shoulder**—the only reason she was making it across the icy lot in one piece.  

Tandstad, **grinning slightly**, **clearly didn’t give a fuck.**

Lifted her head.  

**And burst out laughing.**

She was **damn cold.**  

But more importantly?  

She was **blitzed out of her fucking mind.**  

Jeff, still **staring at her like she had walked out of a literal war zone,** repeated—

Jodi, **eyes unfocused but full of drunken mirth,** **grinned and slurred—**

Bill, **arms crossed, not buying that shit for a second,** squinted.  

**“Define *a little.*”**  

Tandstad, ever helpful, **grinned** and answered **way too fast.**

A beat of silence.  

Then—

Jeremy, openly **gaping.** Jim, **impressed.** Tara, **grinning like she’d just found religion.** Naomi, just **shaking her head slowly, sipping her drink like this was inevitable.**

### **SKYLINE IN THE ARCTIC: TIM & TARA’S CHILI AWAKENING**  

Tara hadn’t been sure about this.  

Tim hadn’t been sure about this.  

Hell, even the **chef**—the tiny Norwegian culinary menace who had made this entire Cincinnati chili experiment happen—**hadn’t been sure about this.**  

But here they were.  

Sitting at a **beautifully set dining table in the middle of a goddamn ice hotel,** slowly eating a dish that had **never before graced this country’s soil.**  

And?  

**It was actually pretty fucking good.**  

Tim took another slow bite, chewing carefully. Tara watched him, her own fork poised halfway to her mouth.  

Neither of them had **expected much.**  

Norwegians didn’t do **spaghetti with chili.** They didn’t do **cinnamon and chocolate in their meat sauce.** And they definitely didn’t do **a goddamn *mountain* of shredded cheddar** dumped on top like a landslide.  

But somehow?  

**It worked.**  

Tara set her fork down and leaned back. **“…Okay, I did not expect this.”**  

Tim, still chewing, nodded. **“Mmm.”** He swallowed, then gestured at his plate. **“This is… actually really fucking good.”**  

The **cheese** had been shredded a little **too finely**, something they’d noticed right away—but it ended up being a blessing in disguise. Instead of **sitting in thick, cold strings like it sometimes did back home,** the cheese had **melted beautifully, folding into the sauce and clinging to the pasta like a perfect, gooey blanket.**  

Tara speared another bite, **watching the chili-slicked noodles twirl around her fork.**  

**“The cinnamon’s subtle,”** she mused. **“And I think she cut down on the clove.”**  

Tim nodded. **“Yeah, she definitely adjusted it. Made it her own.”**  

Tara took the bite. **Warm. Meaty. Cheesy as fuck.** She let out a small, surprised hum. **“…Damn.”**  

Tim smirked. **“Admit it. You didn’t think it’d turn out.”**  

Tara pointed at him with her fork. **“Neither did you.”**  

Tim chuckled, raising his hands in mock surrender. **“Guilty as charged.”**  

The chef, who had been **hovering nearby like an anxious, over-caffeinated hummingbird,** **sprinted forward at full speed.**  

**“DO YOU LIKE IT?!”**  

Tara and Tim both **jumped.**  

Tara barely managed to **catch her fork before it hit the floor.**  

Tim, **still chewing,** held up a finger—**trying to swallow before speaking.**  

Tara, still startled, **gave a slow thumbs-up.** **“…Yeah. It’s really good.”**  

The chef **fucking *squealed* in victory.**  

Then she **slammed her tiny fists on the table.**  

**“I KNEW IT! CINCINNATI CHILI *WORKS!*”**  

Tim, finally recovered, wiped his mouth and chuckled. **“It really does.”**  

The chef **clenched both fists like she had just won an Olympic gold medal.**  

**“I *knew* Americans wouldn’t eat shit food forever! You just needed a Norwegian to fix it!”**  

Tara, laughing, shook her head. **“Okay, let’s not get carried away.”**  

The chef **ignored her completely.**  

She whirled around, clapped her hands, and shouted toward the kitchen—  

**“WE MAKE THIS FOREVER NOW!!”**  

Somewhere in the back, a confused cook called out—  

**“What?! But it’s American!”**  

**“AND?!”**  

Silence. Then—**“…Okay, fine.”**  

Tim leaned toward Tara, muttering, **“I think we just altered the course of Norwegian culinary history.”**  

Tara, smirking, stabbed another bite. **“Yeah, and I’m not mad about it.”**

### **CHILI, CHEESE, AND UNPACKING JODI & JEFF’S UNHINGED SEX LIVES**  

With their plates **half-finished** and their chef now **off somewhere celebrating her new chili empire**, Tara and Tim found themselves **settling in.**  

The **ice hotel dining area** was quiet—at least for now. Most of the band was **off dealing with Jodi’s triumphant, beer-soaked return**, which meant Tara had **Tim all to herself.**  

Not that she was complaining.  

Tim, leaning back in his chair, swirled his drink lazily. **“Okay. Real talk.”**  

Tara arched an eyebrow. **“Uh-oh.”**

Then, with that same **gruff, no-nonsense tone he always carried when it was time to get moving,** he muttered—  

**“Alright. I gotta go.”**  

Tara, **still lying beside him, still warm and settled,** blinked lazily. **“Already?”**  

Tim **grunted, shifting to sit up.** **“Yeah. We’re on a schedule. And I’ll be damned if Madeline gives my chair away at breakfast.”**  

Tara **snorted.** **“Dude, she *will.*”**  

Tim **pointed at her.** **“Exactly. And I am *not* standing around with a fucking plate like an *idiot* because I was too slow getting my ass in gear.”**  

Tara **grinned**, watching him as he stretched, his muscles **tight, defined, still carrying the weight of the night before.**  

Then, after a beat, she **sighed, flopping back against the bed.**  

**“I think I’m gonna skip the studio today.”**  

Tim, **pausing mid-motion, turned to look at her.** **“…Yeah?”**  

Tara **nodded, staring at the ceiling.** **“More or less skip *everything* for a while.”**  

Tim **arched an eyebrow.** **“You that worn out?”**  

Tara **huffed a laugh.** **“Buddy. I got fucked into a *spiritual experience.* I need time to process my new religion.”**  

Tim **chuckled, shaking his head as he reached for his clothes.** **“Jesus Christ, woman.”**  

Tara **grinned.** **“Hey, you’re the one who rewired my brain.”**  

Tim **snorted**, pulling on his shirt. **“Well, enjoy your day off, then. I’ll make sure to eat some extra chili in your honor.”**  

Tara **mock-saluted him from the bed.** **“You’re a true friend.”**  

Tim **winked, smirking.** **“And a *fucking* fantastic lay.”**  

Tara **laughed**, watching him go.  

And for the first time in a long time, she really, truly felt **at ease.**

Her **body?** **Completely wrecked.**  

Her **legs?** **Useless.**  

Her **pussy?** **Annihilated.**  

And yet?  

For the **first time in her life**, she didn’t feel like this was a **walk of shame.**  

No, this was **something else.**  

Something… **victorious.**  

But she *did* need to get back to her room before she fell asleep in **Tim’s bed** and had to explain herself to housekeeping.  

So, **slowly, gingerly,** she **sat up.**  

And immediately **winced.**  

**“…Oh, fuck.”**  

Her **legs were not cooperating.**  

Everything **ached.**  

Her **core muscles had given up on her dreams.**  

She was **definitely waddling back to her room.**

### **THE HALLWAY ENCOUNTER**

**Watching.**  

Like he **knew.**

Jeff **sipped his coffee again.** **“I didn’t say anything.”**  

Tara **huffed, waddling past him.** **“Your face is saying everything.”**  

Jeff, **amused as hell**, leaned against the wall.  

Then, **completely casual—**  

**“Why don’t you try talking to Jodi? She’s still drunk.”**  

Tara **paused mid-waddle.**  

Slowly, she turned her head. **“…Still?”**  

Jeff nodded. **“Still.”**  

Tara sighed, **rubbing her face.**  

**“Of *course* she is.”**  

Jeff **grinned.** **“You got nothing else to do today. Go babysit your girl.”**

**“…If she throws up on me, I’m taking your fucking coffee.”**  

Jeff **smirked.** **“Fair deal.”**  

Tara, **sighing deeply, turned toward Jodi’s room.**  

Time to go **deal with whatever fresh hell was waiting for her there.**

### **THE DRUNKEN HIBERNATION OF JODI**

**“Go on. She’s in there.”**

And immediately?  

She **heard it.**  

**The snoring.**  

Jesus **fuck.**  

It was ***violent.***  

Tara **stared toward the bed**, where Jodi was **completely facedown, starfished across the mattress, dead to the world, snoring like a fucking *chainsaw.*****  

Loud. **Unrelenting.**  

Jeff **leaned against the doorframe, grinning.**  

**“Told you.”**  

Tara, **watching Jodi breathe like she was trying to summon a hurricane,** just shook her head.  

**“…How is she still *alive*?”**  

Jeff **chuckled.** **“Norwegian beer, pure spite, and the will of Odin.”**  

Tara **sighed, rubbing her temples.**

Jeff **sipped his coffee.** **“Yup.”**

This was **her fate.**  

Babysitting **Jodi the Chainsaw.**  

For who the fuck knew **how long.**

Jodi **sighed, then resumed drinking like a scolded toddler.**

Then, after a long pause—

Tara, **still smirking**, took a slow sip of her water and sighed dramatically.

Tara **chuckled.**

**“No, listen!”** Jodi **sat up a little more, eyes narrowing.** **“He’s too old for *Iraq.*”**

Jodi **kept going, pointing vaguely in the air.**  

**“Like—think about it. Iraq kicked off in 2003. What’s Tim, late forties? He would’ve been, what? Fucking *thirty* by then?”**

**“…Oh, *shit*.”**  

Jodi, **nodding like she just cracked a murder case, whispered—**

Tara **stared into the middle distance.**  

Because *fuck*.  

She **didn’t actually know.**  

She knew **he’d served.** He’d mentioned the **Navy.** He’d mentioned the **boiler accident** and how he **tried to save his shipmates.**  

But actual **combat?**

### **WOULD YOU DO IT AGAIN?**  

Jodi, **grinning wickedly, still sprawled out on the bed like a victorious goblin,** turned her head toward Tara.

Tara **froze mid-drink, bottle halfway to her lips.**  

She **blinked.**

She **grinned.**

Tara **grinned wider.** **“Oh, *yeah*.”**

### **HOUSEKEEPING KNOWS WHAT’S UP**  

The **door cracked open** just slightly, and a **housekeeper peeked inside, ready to do her job.**  

But the second she **took in the scene?**  

She **froze.**  

Because sprawled out **dead to the world, tangled in blankets, snoring like absolute menaces**—  

**Were two women.**  

Both looked **wrecked.** **Like they had been through some *shit.***  

Tara was **half on her stomach, arm draped over Jodi’s back, mouth slightly open, breathing deep.**  

Jodi was **flat on her back, hair a complete *disaster*, one leg thrown over the blanket, looking like she had just barely survived a war.**  

And immediately?  

The housekeeper **put it together.**  

That **rich American rockstar guy?** The one with the **gravelly voice, the expensive-ass rooms, the kind of presence that made *everyone* pay attention?**  

He must be **an absolute fucking *animal.***  

Two women, **down for the count, looking like they had been *put through their paces*?**  

**Goddamn.**  

Slowly, carefully—  

She **backed up.**  

Eased the door **shut.**  

And quietly **walked away.**  

She wasn’t about to **mess with whatever legendary recovery was happening in there.**  

---
### **THE VIRAL SPIRAL BEGINS: #WHATDIDJODIDO**  

The **housekeeper didn’t mean to start anything.**  

Really, she didn’t.  

But the second she **stepped into the staff break room,** still **shaking her head in amused disbelief,** she **couldn’t keep it to herself.**  

**“So, you know that rich American rockstar guy? The one with the deep voice and the crazy expensive rooms?”**  

Her coworker, **perking up immediately,** **grinned.**  

**“Jeff?”**  

The housekeeper **nodded.**  

**“Yeah. Well, I just walked into one of the rooms to clean, and there were *two women*—dead asleep, *completely* wiped out. Like, *wrecked*. Looked like they’d been put through *some shit.*”**  

Her coworker **raised an eyebrow.** **“No *way.*”**  

The housekeeper **nodded sagely.** **“Way.”**  

**“Jeff did *that*?”**  

**“Looks like it.”**  

Now, normally, **that would’ve been the end of it.** Just a funny little anecdote. A **“damn, that guy must be *legendary*”** moment.  

But then the coworker, **highly entertained,** went home and **mentioned it to her neighbor.**  

The neighbor?  

**Worked at a bar where some of Jeff’s band had been drinking the night before.**  

And **she’d heard some shit, too.**  

**Something about a woman getting snatched up by the Norwegian military.**  

Which was *weird as fuck.*  

So, naturally, **she told someone else.**  

And *they* told *someone else.*  

And about **three more iterations later—**  

Someone, **somewhere, laughing their ass off, posted the question online:**  

### **#WhatDidJodiDo?**  

And from that moment?  

**It was fucking *on.***

---

### **THE STRUGGLE OF POLISHED ICE**  

Jodi was **sleeping beautifully.**  

Warm. **Cozy.** Deep in a **post-debauchery coma.**  

Until—  

**“Get the fuck up.”**  

Jodi **grunted.**  

Something **shook her.**  

**“Come *on,* I’m bored.”**  

Jodi **blinked groggily, turning her head just enough to see Naomi standing over her, arms crossed, looking way too awake for whatever ungodly hour this was.**  

Jodi, **voice hoarse, grumbled,** **“Fuck *off.”***  

Naomi **rolled her eyes.** **“No. You *reek.*”**  

Jodi **snorted.** **“That’s how you wake me up? *Insult me?*”**  

Naomi **shrugged.** **“Would you prefer I set you on fire?”**  

Jodi **groaned, rubbing her face.**  

**“…I do kind of reek, though.”**  

Naomi **nodded.** **“Yeah. So, let’s go. Shower. Now.”**  

Before Jodi could **argue,** Naomi **grabbed the blanket, ripped it off, and started dragging her ass out of bed.**  

**“GET WITH IT. BE SNAPPY.”**  

Jodi, **grumbling murderously,** stumbled to her feet, still **half-asleep, half-dying, and fully regretting every choice she’d made yesterday.**  

### **COMMUNAL SHOWERS: THE STRUGGLE CONTINUES**  

The **walk down the hall was hell.**  

Jodi was **sore as fuck.**  

Not from **drinking.** Not from **partying.**  

**From that goddamn helo ride.**  

Every **muscle in her body** was **paying the price** for getting yanked out of the sky like a **tactical dumbass.**  

Her shoulders? **Destroyed.**  

Her back? **Fucked.**  

Her thighs? **Absolutely obliterated.**  

She **was gonna pay for this shit for days.**  

Naomi, **completely unfazed, strutted into the communal showers like she owned the place.**  

Jodi, **dragging behind, grumbled,** **“I feel like I got run over by a *fucking* tank.”**  

Naomi **turned on the water.** **“You basically did. Now shut up and get in.”**  

Jodi **sighed, stepped under the water, and—**  

**FROZE.**  

**“OH FUCK THAT’S COLD.”**  

Naomi **cackled, already lathering up.** **“That’s what you get for being slow.”**
