Her **shoulders were stiff as hell.**  

Even just **lifting her arms to scrub herself** felt like she was trying to **bench press a helicopter.**  

Jodi **groaned, muttering,** **“This *sucks.*”**  

Naomi, **glancing over, raised an eyebrow.** **“You struggling?”**  

Jodi **gritted her teeth.** **“…Yes.”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“You want me to do it for you?”**  

Jodi **glared.** **“Bitch, no.”**  

Naomi **chuckled.** **“Suit yourself.”**  

Jodi, **muttering under her breath,** went back to **struggling her way through the most painful shower of her life.**  

This?  

This was **gonna be a *long* fucking day.**  

---

### **THE WALK OF EXHAUSTION & BRA-RELATED DEFEAT**  

Jodi, **clean but still wrecked as hell,** dragged herself **back to her room**, her muscles **protesting every step.**  

Naomi **walked beside her,** casual as ever, **not suffering even a fraction of what Jodi was.**  

Jodi hated her a little for that.  

As soon as they entered, Jodi **paused, blinking.**  

Because Tara?  

**Was dead the fuck asleep.**  

Sprawled on the bed, **face half-buried in a pillow, breathing slow and deep, looking like she had not moved in hours.**  

Naomi, **glancing at her, shrugged.** **“Not gonna ask. Not gonna judge.”**  

Jodi **sighed heavily, rubbing her face.**  

**“Tara fucked *all night* with Tim and skipped sleeping.”**  

Naomi, **pausing for a beat, processed that.**  

Then, in a completely **flat, vaguely disappointed tone—**  

**“…Oh.”**  

Jodi **groaned, stomping over to her bag.** **“What does *that* mean?”**  

Naomi, **completely neutral, shrugged.** **“Nothing.”**  

Jodi **squinted.** **“You’re lying.”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“It’s just—”** she **tilted her head.** **“You know. *Tim.*”**  

Jodi **rolled her eyes.** **“Yeah, yeah. Mutant cock. Can’t come. Needs a therapy session after sex. Heard it all.”**  

Naomi **snickered.** **“That’s not *exactly* what I meant, but sure.”**  

Jodi, **grumbling, yanked her bra out of her bag and attempted to put it on.**  

And **immediately struggled.**  

Her **arms were still too sore.**  

Her **shoulders fucking refused.**  

The second she **tried to twist her arms back to clasp the damn thing—**  

**Agony.**  

Jodi **hissed, defeated, and hung her head.**  

**“…I need help.”**  

Naomi **grinned, stepping over.** **“Babe. You are *so* fucked up from that helo ride.”**  

Jodi, **gritting her teeth,** **“Just hook me up before I throw myself into traffic.”**  

Naomi **quickly did up the clasps**, **snapping the band a little for good measure.**  

Jodi **glared.** **“Bitch.”**  

Naomi **beamed.** **“You’re welcome.”**  

Jodi **sighed, adjusting her straps.** **“God, I need a massage.”**  

Naomi **tilted her head, thoughtful.** **“You know, tonight would be a good night to soak in the steam bath and detoxify.”**  

Jodi **paused.**  

Then slowly **turned her head, squinting.**  

**“…Naomi.”**  

Naomi **blinked innocently.** **“What?”**  

Jodi **pointed at her.** **“That was some *granola crunchy lib* bullshit right there.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Babe. You drank *Norwegian* beer last night. You need a *spiritual reset*.”**  

Jodi **groaned loudly.** **“Oh my *God.*”**  

Naomi, **smirking, patted her shoulder.** **“Just accept the woo-woo and let yourself *heal*, babe.”**  

Jodi, **fully done with this conversation, flopped back onto the bed.**  

**“Wake me up when I’ve turned into fucking *Gwyneth Paltrow.*”**  

Naomi **laughed, already heading for the door.** **“Fine, but only if I get to light some sage first.”**  

Jodi, **muffled into the pillow—**  

**“*Fuck off, Naomi.*”**  

---

### **THE ENERGY CRISIS OF JODI**  

Jodi, **still lying flat on the bed, barely clinging to life,** lifted her head just enough to give Naomi a **wan, exhausted smile.**  

She was **trying.**  

Really, she was.  

Trying to be **energetic. Trying to show appreciation.**  

But, Jesus **fuck.**  

It was a **lot.**  

Naomi, **watching her struggle, smirked.**  

**“Babe. You look like you just fought the entire Norwegian military.”**  

Jodi, **muffled into the pillow,** grunted, **“I *did*.”**  

Naomi **laughed, shaking her head, already pulling out her phone.**  

**“Alright, you useless bitch. Let me at least figure out when we can get into town.”**  

She **called down to the front desk**, waiting while some **cheerful Norwegian concierge answered in that disgustingly chipper morning tone.**  

Jodi, **watching from the bed, groaned.**  

Naomi **snapped her fingers at her.** **“Hydrate, Polished Ice. You’re still half pickled.”**  

Jodi **flipped her off weakly.**  

Naomi, **grinning, spoke into the phone.** **“Hi, can you tell me when the next sleigh into town is running?”**  

There was a **brief pause,** then Naomi **nodded.**  

**“Uh-huh. Uh-huh. Yep, that works. Great, thanks.”**  

She **hung up, turned back to Jodi, and smirked.**  

**“Alright. We have a ride in forty-five minutes. So *move your ass.*”**  

Jodi **groaned dramatically, burying her face into the mattress.**  

Naomi **arched an eyebrow.**  

**“Not all of us get *dropped off at the front door by a freaking *helicopter, Jodi!*”**  

Jodi, **laughing weakly into the pillow, waved a hand.** **“Privilege. It’s *so* hard.”**  

Naomi **rolled her eyes.**  

**“Bitch, get dressed.”**

---

### **THE MID-MORNING SLEIGH RIDE: DARK, COLD, AND NOT ROMANTIC AT ALL**  

Jodi **huddled deeper into her coat**, watching the **endless stretch of Arctic darkness** as the sleigh **cut through the wilderness.**  

Fifteen minutes of this.  

Fifteen minutes of **absolute pitch black, biting cold, and snow crunching loudly beneath the runners.**  

It was **beautiful.**  

It was **quiet.**  

It would be **romantic as fuck if Jeff was here.**  

Instead?  

She was **clutching her coat tighter, hoping to God the SUV was already heated when they finally reached civilization.**  

Naomi, **seated next to her, completely unfazed by the frigid air,** exhaled slowly and murmured,  

**“You know, if you weren’t dying, this would be kind of nice.”**  

Jodi **grunted.** **“If I wasn’t dying, I’d be in bed.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Fair.”**  

They rode on, the sleigh **gliding smoothly through the snow, the only sounds their breath, the muffled jingle of harness bells, and the occasional snap of a tree branch under the weight of ice.**  

It was **still too early, too dark, too fucking cold.**  

Jodi **sighed, breath fogging in the air.**  

**“How much longer?”**  

Naomi checked her phone. **“About five more minutes.”**  

Jodi **closed her eyes briefly, muttering,** **“Please, God, let the car be warm.”**  

Naomi **smirked.** **“Maybe if you pray hard enough, Jeff will be in there waiting for you with a blanket.”**  

Jodi **opened one eye.**  

Then, **deadpan—**  

**“If Jeff is waiting for me with a *heated seat* and a *thermos of coffee*, I’ll blow him in the parking lot.”**  

Naomi **fucking wheezed.**  

**“Jesus *Christ*, Jodi.”**  

Jodi **sighed dramatically.** **“I *deserve* warmth, Naomi.”**  

Naomi **laughed the rest of the way down the trail.**

---

### **THE MYTH VS. THE REALITY OF RECORDING MUSIC**  

By the time the **sleigh finally arrived at the road**, Jodi and Naomi **climbed stiffly into the waiting SUV**, **blessing whatever kind soul had already blasted the heat.**  

No **Jeff.** No **thermos of coffee.** No **blowjobs in the parking lot.**  

Just **warm seats and a silent, Norwegian driver who clearly did not care about their suffering.**  

Jodi **sighed in relief.** **“Okay, fine. I’m not blowing anyone, but I *am* gonna take a nap on the drive.”**  

Naomi **chuckled.** **“You’ve earned it, babe.”**  

Jodi **closed her eyes.**  

And then?  

They were **off to the studio.**  

---

### **WELCOME TO THE MOST BORING FORM OF LOUD**  

By the time they arrived, the band had already been **hard at work for hours.**  

Jodi and Naomi **slipped in quietly**, **making their way into the control room**, where Jeff, Avril, and the others were **listening intently to yet another playback.**  

And **within ten minutes?**  

Jodi **fully understood Jeff’s warning.**  

Recording?  

Was **fucking bizarre.**  

It was either **insanely loud—**an explosion of drums, bass, guitars, vocals—**or it was absolutely nothing.**  

Just **endless waiting.**  

Jeff had explained it to her before, but it had always sounded so **glamorous.** The idea of **writing music, then recording it, producing it, bringing it to life.**  

But in **reality?**  

It was **hours of playing the same goddamn take over and over.**  

It was **tiny adjustments.** **Tweak the drum tone. Change the mix on the bass. Try a different vocal approach.**  

And after **watching them loop through the same chorus for what felt like an eternity**, Jodi **muttered under her breath—**  

**“This is the *opposite* of how I thought the music industry worked.”**  

Naomi, **watching too, arms crossed, smirked.** **“What, you thought they just played it once and it was done?”**  

Jodi **narrowed her eyes.** **“I thought it would be *cooler.*”**  

Jeff, **without turning around, muttered—**  

**“Told you.”**  

Jodi **exhaled, dropping into a chair.**  

It was going to be **a *long* fucking day.**  

---

### **THE STUDIO GRIND: SMALL MOMENTS & SCRUFFY FRINGES**  

Jodi, **still exhausted, still processing the sheer mind-numbing repetition of music production,** barely registered movement in the recording booth—  

Until **Avril glanced up, caught her eye, and… actually smiled.**  

It was **small. Brief.** But definitely **real.**  

Jodi blinked.  

Avril, **casually raising a hand, gave a tiny, friendly wave**, then gestured something **vague but familiar.**  

That **little flick of the wrist.**  

That **“shit sucks, but we’re powering through” kind of motion.**  

And Jodi realized—  

Avril looked **just as fried as she felt.**  

That same **glassed-out exhaustion.**  

But at the same time, **she was still giving as good as she got.**  

Still **putting in the work. Still pushing through.**  

Jodi found herself **begrudgingly respecting that.**  

Then, from the booth, **Jim stood up from behind his drum kit, stretched, and made his way into the control room.**  

Jodi **watched him go, noticing something immediately.**  

The dude was **letting his facial hair go.**  

Just **a little scruff. A touch of fringe along his jaw.**  

And instantly?  

Jodi **felt that in her fucking soul.**  

Because **when she got too lazy or too busy to shave her legs?**  

Yeah.  

That **exact same uneven, awkward bullshit happened to her.**  

Jodi, **half-conscious, muttered under her breath—**  

**“Damn, Jim. I see your struggle.”**  

Naomi, **grinning, glanced at her.** **“What?”**  

Jodi **waved a tired hand at Jim.** **“Shaving. Too much work. I get it.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Babe, you are so fucking *gone* right now.”**  

Jodi **sighed deeply, slumping in her chair.**  

**“Wake me up when they do something *different*.”**  

Naomi **laughed and turned back to the booth.**  

It was going to be a **long-ass** recording session.

---

### **THE SLEEPY STUDIO SESSION: SOFT SOUNDS & STUBBORN DRUMMERS**  

Jodi, **half-conscious in her chair**, let the slow, **subtle rhythm of the studio lull her into that weird, floaty space between awake and asleep.**  

It wasn’t the **hard-hitting, wall-of-sound rock shit she was used to hearing from them.**  

This one?  

**Soft. Stripped down.**  

Avril was **on the piano**, her **fingers gliding over the keys in something low and steady.**  

Jer was **picking lightly at an acoustic guitar, the sound delicate but intentional.**  

And Jeff?  

**Either not playing at all, or just tapping one note on the bass so subtly it barely registered.**  

Which was **weird as hell.**  

Jeff on a guitar? **Loud. Complex. Ruthless.**  

Jeff on a bass? **Apparently a fucking ninja.**  

But Jim?  

Jim was being **fussy as hell.**  

The **gated reverb on his drums wasn’t giving him what he wanted,** and he was **getting frustrated.**  

Jodi, **half-listening, barely awake, heard the murmured conversation in the control room.**  

Jim, **grumbling**—**“It’s not *punching* right. It’s too dry. I need *air* in it, but it keeps coming out flat.”**  

Jeff, **sounding completely unbothered**—**“Then compress the tail and tweak the EQ. You’re getting room noise you don’t like.”**  

Jim, **grunting, adjusting some settings, trying another hit.**  

Same result. **Still wrong.**  

Jodi, **in that dreamy, nearly-asleep state,** just thought—  

**Jesus. If they’re gonna be this boring, I might actually get a nap in.**  

And with that?  

She **let herself drift.**  

---
### **CASSIOPEIA A & THE STUDIO TRICKERY**  

Jodi was **somewhere between napping and listening**, floating in that **perfect, half-conscious state where the music wasn’t quite real, but wasn’t quite a dream either.**  

Soft piano. **Gentle guitar.** The **occasional frustrated grunt from Jim, still fighting his damn drum settings.**  

Then—  

Naomi’s **voice cut through the haze.**  

**“Tim, can you do that trick again with the display and show the lyrics? I’m *so* lost.”**  

Jodi **cracked an eye open**, just in time to see Tim, who had been **leaning back in his chair, watching everything with the calm patience of a man who had survived far worse than studio bullshit,** **chuckle and reach for the console.**  

**“Yeah, babe, I got you.”**  

A few **clicks, a flick of a switch—**  

And suddenly, the **big screen in the control room switched over.**  

Lyrics. **Projected large.**  

Jodi, **still groggy, let her eyes adjust, scanning the text.**  

At the top?  

**A title.**  

**Cassiopeia A.**  

Jodi **blinked, frowning slightly.**  

She knew the guys had a **thing** for **overly precious, hidden-meaning song titles.**  

Jeff, in particular, **got off on naming shit after obscure references.**  

But **this one?**  

She knew she’d **heard it before.**  

Something **about space. Astronomy. A star?**  

Still half-asleep, she let the words **roll around in her brain**, wondering—  

**What the hell does this one *mean*?**  

---

### **CONCEPT ALBUMS & OLD GRUDGES**  

Jodi, **blinking the last remnants of sleep from her eyes,** frowned at the screen, her brain **slowly piecing things together.**  

Cassiopeia A.  

**A concept album?**  

She barely had time to process that before Tim, **casually as hell,** confirmed it.  

**“Yeah, they’re assembling a concept album.”**  

Jodi **immediately sat up, her exhaustion shoved aside by pure instinctual alarm.**  

Because she **remembered something.**  

From **way back in the day.**  

One of **Jeff’s old managers—loud, dramatic, prone to drinking way too much whiskey—used to go on *legendary* rants about this exact topic.**  

**“NO CONCEPT ALBUMS. NONE. YOU ARE NOT *RUSH!* YOU ARE NOT *THE FUCKING WHO!* WRITE *SINGLES!* MAKE *HITS!* STOP GETTING *WEIRD!*”**  

And now?  

Now they were **making a goddamn concept album?**  

Jodi **turned to Tim, narrowing her eyes.** **“Does Jeff not *remember* the absolute *shitstorm* his band manager used to throw over this?”**  

Tim, **completely unfazed, shrugged.** **“Oh, he remembers.”**  

Jodi **stared.** **“…And?”**  

Tim **smirked.** **“And he doesn’t give a fuck.”**  

Jodi **sighed loudly, rubbing her temples.** **“Of course he doesn’t.”**  

Then, something **clicked.**  

She turned back to Tim, suspicion creeping in. **“Wait. Who the hell *talked him into this?*”**  

Tim, **grinning, leaned back in his chair.**  

**“Avril.”**  

Jodi **froze.**  

Then immediately?  

She **hated it.**  

Not **because of the concept album thing.**  

Not **because of the inevitable pretentious bullshit that was sure to follow.**  

But because **it was Avril’s idea.**  

And Jodi, **as a matter of principle,** was **predisposed to fucking hate anything Avril thought up.**  

She crossed her arms.  

**“…This is gonna piss me off, isn’t it?”**  

Tim **grinned wider.**  

**“Oh, babe. *So much.*”**  

---

### **BLOODY HELL, AVRIL. REALLY?**  

Jodi, **still trying to wake up, still trying to wrap her head around this concept album bullshit,** squinted at the lyrics on the screen.  

From what she could tell, it was **a little poetic, a little moody, maybe a bit raunchy—but nothing wildly out of place for them.**  

So she muttered, **half to herself—**  

**“I mean… sounds a bit raunchy, but nothing *unusual.*”**  

Tim, **grinning like he had a secret,** took a sip of his drink.  

Then, **casually as fuck—**  

**“It’s actually adapted from a piece of erotic fiction.”**  

Jodi **froze.**  

Her brain **stalled out.**  

She turned her head **slowly, like she was trying to make sure she actually heard that right.**  

**“…The *fuck* did you just say?”**  

Tim, **fully enjoying this, smirked.** **“It’s erotic fiction. The story they’re pulling from.”**  

Jodi **blinked once. Then twice.**  

Then she **sighed deeply, rubbing her face.**  

**“…Bloody *hell*, Avril. *Really?*”**  

Tim **grinned wider.** **“Oh yeah.”**  

Jodi **dropped her hands, groaned, and flopped back into her chair.**  

**“I *knew* I was gonna hate this.”**  

Naomi, **listening with interest, finally piped up.** **“So wait… they’re making a *concept album* based on a *porn story?*”**  

Tim **shrugged.** **“Not *exactly* porn. But *definitely* erotica.”**  

Jodi **groaned again.** **“For *fuck’s* sake.”**  

Tim, **grinning at her misery, leaned back.** **“Told you, babe. You were *so* gonna hate this.”**  

---

### **BRACE FOR IMPACT: THE SYNTH THAT SHOOK THE EARTH**  

Tim, **grinning like an absolute menace,** suddenly sat up and shouted—  

**“BRACE! BRACE! BRACE!”**  

Jodi barely had time to process **why the hell he was yelling like a Navy pilot about to crash-land** before—  

**The band hit verse three.**  

And suddenly?  

**The entire goddamn building shook.**  

Jodi **flinched**, **heart lurching**, every nerve in her body **instantly on high alert.**  

It wasn’t even Jeff.  

At least—**it *should’ve* been Jeff.**  

Because Jeff, when he really leaned into the bass, could **make entire rooms vibrate**, could **rattle glass in its frame.**  

But Jodi, **suddenly second-guessing every law of physics she thought she knew,** realized—  

**It *wasn’t* Jeff.**  

No, all that **insane, scything, borderline-unholy sound** was coming from—  

**Bill.**  

From that **tiny little keyboard in front of him.**  

His synthesizer, for lack of a better description, sounded like **God’s fucking *lawnmower.***  
Jodi’s **eyes widened.**  

Her **entire skeleton** was vibrating.  

If she hadn’t been wearing a **headset**, she might have actually **gone insane.**  

Because it wasn’t even **a complex melody.**  

**Four notes. Three times in a row.**  

That was it.  

And yet—  

**It *scythed through the space-time continuum.***  

It was **bombastic. It was absurd.**  

It was **so over-the-top that her first instinct was to burst into laughter.**  

Instead, she just **gawked at Tim, who was grinning like a madman.**  

**“Holy *shit*, Tim.”**  

Tim, **watching her reaction with pure delight, just shrugged.**  

**“Told you.”**  

---

### **THE BLADDER-SHAKING SUPERSONIC SYNTH**  

Naomi, **wide-eyed, shifting slightly in her seat,** blurted out—  

**“I *felt* that in my *bladder!*”**  

Jodi, **still recovering, still feeling her *bones* resonate from the absurdity of Bill’s synthesizer,** could only nod.  

**“Yeah. *Same.*”**  

And yet—  

In the booth?  

**The band looked fucking *giddy*.**  

Jeff, **normally cool and controlled, was *grinning*.**  

Bill, **completely unfazed by the *chaos* he’d just unleashed, adjusted a setting on his tiny keyboard like he wasn’t a *goddamn war criminal.***  

Jim, **the fussiest man alive, actually nodded in approval.**  

And Avril?  

Avril just **fucking smirked.**  

Jodi, **bewildered, gestured vaguely at the scene.** **“Why do these *crazy* people look so *pleased* with themselves?”**  

Tim, **grinning like he lived for moments like this,** leaned forward and said—  

**“Cassiopeia A.”**  

Jodi **squinted.** **“…The song title?”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yeah. You know what that actually *is?*”**  

Jodi **shrugged.** **“A constellation?”**  

Tim **grinned wider.** **“A *supernova remnant*.”**  

Jodi **blinked.**  

Tim, **clearly enjoying himself, continued.**  

**“Cassiopeia A was probably the *biggest* supernova in our galaxy in the last ten thousand years. It exploded so *bright* that, if you were alive back then, you could’ve seen it in the sky *during the day.*”**  

Jodi **raised an eyebrow.** **“Yeah?”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yeah. And the *craziest* part? Scientists *discovered* it the day after they invented *radio astronomy.*”**  

Naomi, **still looking rattled, frowned.** **“Wait. What?”**  

Tim **leaned back, hands behind his head.**  

**“They build a radio telescope, turn it on, and *immediately* pick up a signal from the *boom* still echoing through space. The moment they tried listening? Cassiopeia A was *already* screaming at them.”**  

Jodi, **processing that, glanced back at the band.**  

Then back at the lyrics.  

Then, finally, back at Tim.  

**“…So they’re trying to make this song *sound like a fucking supernova?***”  

Tim, **grinning, spread his hands.**  

**“Sounds like it *worked,* doesn’t it?”**  

Naomi **groaned, rubbing her temples.**  

**“No *wonder* my bladder nearly exploded.”**  

Jodi, **deadpan, exhaled slowly.**  

**“Bloody fucking hell, Avril. *Really?***”**  

---

### **CASSIOPEIA A: THE SUPERNOVA BLOWJOB ANTHEM**  

Jodi, **still trying to process the fact that the band was actively trying to sonically re-create a goddamn *supernova*,** turned back to Tim, still **mildly horrified.**  

And then?  

Tim, **casual as ever,** smirked and said—  

**“Yeah, this is all about a blowjob.”**  

Jodi **froze.**  

Naomi **made a strangled noise.**  

Tim, **grinning like the absolute menace he was,** gave a knowing laugh.  

**“Oh yeah. They’re gonna alternate between being *subtle* and *unsubtle* the entire damn time.”**  

Jodi, **blinking hard, turned back to the lyrics.**  

Cassiopeia A.  

A fucking **star explosion.**  

That you could **see in daylight.**  

And this whole song was **a glorified deep-throating metaphor?**  

**Jesus *Christ.* Avril. *Really?***  

Before she could fully unpack that nightmare, Tim gestured toward the recording booth, **tilting his chin at Jeremy.**  

**“Speaking of Avril… Look at Jeremy.”**  

Jodi **squinted through the glass.**  

Jeremy, **fingers moving delicately over his acoustic guitar, was locked in.**  

Fully **engrossed. Dialed in. Brow furrowed in intense focus.**  

Tim **chuckled.** **“The man is *jealous* as fuck about crafting his guitar parts.”**  

Jodi **raised an eyebrow.** **“Jealous? Of *what?*”**  

Tim, **grinning, pointed at Jeff.**  

**“Of *him.*”**  

Jodi **glanced at Jeff—**  

And **saw it immediately.**  

Jeff, **cool as ever, playing effortlessly, adjusting things on the fly, completely unfazed by the entire ridiculous process.**  

Meanwhile, **Jeremy was killing himself to get things right.**  

Jodi **huffed a quiet laugh.** **“Damn. Jer’s in the driver’s seat on this one, huh?”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yep. And you *missed* the absolute *donnybrook* between those two yesterday.”**  

Jodi, **immediately invested, turned to him.**  

**“Oh, *fuck off.* Tell me everything.”**  

Tim **grinned wider.**  

**“Babe. You *would not* believe the shit they got into.”**  

---

### **THE DONNYBROOK: WHEN BROTHERS BICKER LIKE IDIOTS**  

Tim, **grinning, shaking his head at the memory,** leaned back in his chair.  

**“Oh, babe. Things *deteriorated* fast.”**  

Jodi, **already smirking,** **crossed her arms.** **“Define ‘deteriorated.’”**  

Tim **grinned.** **“Full meltdown. *Precious* insults. Shit got *personal.*”**  

Naomi, **who had been quietly taking this all in, finally perked up.** **“Wait. Jeff and Jeremy actually *fought*?”**  

Tim **chuckled.** **“Not *physically.* Just *aggressively fucking stupid.*”**  

Jodi **snorted.** **“Like what? ‘Your tone sucks?’ ‘Your timing’s off?’”**  

Tim **grinned wider.**  

**“Nah, babe. They started insulting each other’s *mother.*”**  

Jodi **blinked.**  

Then frowned.  

Then frowned *harder.*  

**“…Wait. Aren’t they, like…  born *18 months apart?***”  

Tim **shrugged.** **“Something like that. I’m not for sure.”**  

Jodi **stared.** **“So… they were literally insulting *the same woman.*”**  

Tim **laughed.** **“Oh, yeah. And *didn’t let details stop them.*”**  

Jodi **shook her head in absolute disbelief.** **“Jesus *Christ.*”**  

Tim **sighed dramatically.** **“Poor Avril got dragged into it, too.”**  

Jodi **arched an eyebrow.** **“How the hell did *she* get involved?”**  

Tim **grinned.** **“She tried to *mediate.*”**  

Jodi **burst out laughing.** **“Oh, that was her *first mistake.*”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yeah. The second mistake was opening her mouth at all, because Jeremy *immediately* turned on her and started bitching about how her vocal harmonies were stepping on his guitar lines.”**  

Naomi **gasped, deeply entertained.** **“No *way.*”**  

Tim **chuckled.** **“Oh, *way.* And Jeff—*who had already been fighting with Jeremy for an hour*—jumped *right* back in and started yelling about how Jeremy was *the worst fucking diva in the room,* which was saying something because Avril was *literally there.*”**  

Jodi **slapped a hand over her mouth, wheezing.**  

Naomi **leaned forward.** **“Holy shit. Who broke it up?”**  

Tim **sighed.** **“Jim.”**  

Jodi **winced.** **“That poor bastard.”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yeah. Had to stand up, slam his drumsticks down, and tell everyone to *shut the fuck up* before they ruined another take.”**  

Jodi, **still laughing, shook her head.** **“God, I wish I’d seen that.”**  

Tim **smirked.** **“Oh, babe. I *wish* I had footage.”**  

Jodi **grinned, sitting back.** **“So what I’m hearing is… nothing’s changed.”**  

Tim **laughed.** **“Nope. Not a fucking thing.”**

---

### **AVRIL: LOST PUPPY OR SECRET WEAPON?**  

Tim, **arms crossed, speaking like a man who had seen some shit,** exhaled slowly.  

**"Biggest surprise these last few days? How chill and professional Avril's been."**  

Jodi, **already squinting suspiciously,** **shifted in her seat.**  

She **knew** where this was going.  

Tim, **catching her expression, lifted a hand.**  

**"I *know* what your opinion is. No disrespect. But, babe… you're *wrong.*"**  

Jodi, **jaw tightening, started to respond, but Tim just kept talking.**  

**"Avril was the *right* pick for this. Even if Jeff was thinking with his dick? His dick was *right*."**  

Jodi **made an offended noise.** **"Oh, *fuck off.*"**  

Naomi, **grinning, leaned in.** **"No, no, keep going. This is *great.*"**  

Tim **grinned, shaking his head.**  

**"The funny thing is—half the time, she looks like a lost puppy. Like one of those dogs left outside a store, just *waiting* for someone to take her home, but no one does."**  

Jodi **rolled her eyes so hard she nearly gave herself a headache.**  

Tim **ignored her and kept going.**  

**"She's chill. She's earnest. She's hard-working. She's inventive—"**  

**"She's a *cunt!*"** Jodi **interrupted, exasperated.**  

Tim, **unfazed, just sipped his coffee.**  

Naomi, **laughing her ass off, clapped her hands.**  

**"Oh my *God*, Jodi. Just say you hate her and go."**  

Jodi, **glaring at both of them, muttered,** **"I *have* said that. Many times."**  

Tim, **grinning wider, leaned forward.**  

**"Yeah, babe. And *you're still wrong.*"**  

---

### **THE MOLLY REVELATION**  

Naomi, **leaning back in her chair, clearly enjoying the moment,** suddenly announced—  

**“So. I’ve got a *huge* factoid. May or may not be relevant.”**  

Tim and Jodi **both turned to her immediately.**  

Naomi **held up a hand.** **“But. It has to stay a secret.”**  

Jodi **narrowed her eyes.** **“If you’re about to tell me Avril’s a lizard person, I swear to God—”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“No, babe. But I *was* in the sauna with her last night.”**  

Tim’s **eyebrows shot up.**  

**“…The *fuck?***”  

Jodi, **immediately irked, crossed her arms.**  

**“Why?”**  

Naomi **shrugged.** **“Because she was *there*? And I was *there*? And we had a *swell conversation?***”  

Jodi **rolled her eyes.**  

Tim, **grinning, leaned forward.** **“Okay, but *how naked* were we talking?”**  

Jodi **slapped his arm.** **“*Focus.*”**  

Naomi **ignored them both.**  

**“Anyway, after we talked for a bit, she invited me up to her room.”**  

Jodi, **suspicious as hell, squinted.** **“And?”**  

Naomi **smiled innocently.** **“She offered me some Molly.”**  

Instantly?  

**Silence.**  

Tim and Jodi **both went *dead still.***  

Tim **blinked.**  

Jodi, **in a completely calm, *neutral* voice,** turned to Naomi and asked—  

**“…One. Do you actually understand what Molly *is?***”  

Naomi **rolled her eyes.** **“Babe. My mom’s a *pastor*. I know all about it.”**  

Tim **exhaled, shaking his head.** **“Jesus Christ.”**  

Jodi **was not done.**  

**“…Two. Were you *stupid enough* to try it?”**  

Naomi **gave her an unimpressed look.**  

**“Jodi. I have *literally* spent my entire life watching my mom deal with parishioners’ drug habits. I am *not* stupid.”**  

Jodi **let out a slow breath, nodding.** **“Okay. Good.”**  

Then, after a pause, she frowned.  

**“Wait. So if you *didn’t* take it… why the hell are you telling us this?”**  

Naomi **smirked.**  

**“Because now you’re wondering *if Avril did.*”**  

Jodi’s **stomach sank.**  

Tim, **leaning back, rubbing his jaw, sighed.**  

**“…Oh, *fuck.*”**  

---

### **THE MOLLY MICRODOSING REVELATION**  

Naomi, **clearly enjoying how much this was messing with them,** leaned forward and said,  

**“Relax. Avril’s got a *prescription.*”**  

Tim and Jodi, **in perfect synchronization,** both snapped their heads toward her and—  

**“WHAT. THE. EVER-LOVING. *HELL?!***”**  

Naomi, **completely unbothered, lifted a hand.** **“I *also* learned a new word last night: *microdosing.*”**  

Jodi, **blinking rapidly, struggling to keep up, just shook her head.** **“Micro—*what?!*”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“Yeah. Apparently, it’s legal in some of Canada.”**  

Tim, **grumbling, rubbing his temples, muttered,** **“That *explains* so much.”**  

Naomi **shrugged.** **“Or at least, it’s partly legal in the only part of Canada that *matters*—the *GTA.*”**  

Jodi **covered her face with both hands, inhaled deeply, and exhaled through her nose.**  

Then, muffled, she groaned—  

**“Oh, *fuck* me running. Avril’s *medically* rolling?”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Yep.”**  

Tim, **now genuinely intrigued, tilted his head.** **“Okay, hold the fuck up. You’re telling me she’s *prescribed* Molly?”**  

Naomi **nodded.** **“Yep.”**  

Jodi, **finally looking up, stared hard at Naomi.**  

**“…*By who?* The *Canadian Ministry of Bangers & Vibes?***”  

Naomi **fucking *cackled.***  

Tim, **grinning, muttered,** **“Christ. No wonder she’s been so *chill.*”**  

Jodi, **groaning again, collapsed back in her chair.**  

**“I *knew* I was gonna hate this.”**  

Naomi **just smiled sweetly.**  

**“Told you. *Huge* factoid.”**  

---

### **IS AVRIL ACTUALLY DIFFERENT?**  

Jodi, **head resting against the back of her chair, staring up at the ceiling, let her brain start turning over the facts.**  

Did it **make a difference?**  

Was that why Avril was **so damn chill now?**  

She glanced over at Tim, **brow furrowing slightly.**  

**"How long have you known her? Like, *closely*?"**  

Tim, **tilting his head, considering, finally shrugged.**  

**"Probably three months, give or take a day."**  

Jodi **blinked.** **“That’s it?”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“I wasn’t around for the 2013 album she worked on with them. That was before my time.”**  

Jodi **exhaled slowly.**  

Tim, **leaning back, arms crossed, then added—**  

**“And, actually… I’ve been on again, off again considering the same thing. For my PTSD.”**  

Jodi’s **head snapped toward him.** **“*You?*”**  

Tim **nodded, completely unfazed.** **“Yeah. Looked into it. Read the studies. Talked to a few guys who tried it.”**  

Naomi, **suddenly more serious, asked,** **“What stopped you?”**  

Tim **sighed, rubbing his jaw.**  

**“My brain chemistry is *already* frazzled as fuck. Last thing I wanna do is rattle it *more* and make my episodes worse.”**  

Jodi **nodded slowly.** **That actually made sense.**  

Tim, **watching Avril through the glass, smirked slightly.**  

**“But after watching *her* work? Might be something to socialized medicine.”**  

Jodi, **snorting, shook her head.** **“Christ, Tim.”**  

Tim **grinned.** **“What? Just saying. Maybe Canada’s got this one right.”**  

Naomi, **laughing, shrugged.** **“I mean, if we can get *Avril fucking Lavigne* mellowed out, maybe they’re onto something.”**  

Jodi, **grumbling, muttered,** **“Still a cunt.”**  

Tim **laughed.** **“Babe, I *know.*”**

---

### **THE BIG BOYS’ TABLE OR BUST**  

The band **finally** broke for lunch, and Jodi **immediately knew where she was sitting.**  

She didn’t even have to think about it.  

She **belonged** at the big boys’ table.  

And if **Madeline—Jeff’s terrifyingly competent assistant—** didn’t have a chair set aside for her?  

Then Jodi would **simply slide her panties off, straddle Jeff right then and there, and use *his* chair.**  

Tim, **chuckling, shaking his head, muttered—**  

**“I heard they’re having roast beef sandwiches and roasted broccoli.”**  

Jodi **groaned loudly, throwing her head back.**  

**“Oh, *fuck me.* That’s *definitely* Jeff’s doing.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Babe, how do you know?”**  

Jodi **gestured vaguely, exhausted.**  

**“Because the man is *weirdly* obsessed with roasted broccoli. It’s one of his *top five* favorite foods.”**  

Naomi **blinked.** **“…Wait. *Seriously?*”**  

Tim, **grinning, nodded.** **“Oh yeah. He gets *personally offended* when people say they don’t like it.”**  

Jodi **sighed dramatically.**  

**“It’s like a *personality trait* for him. Jeff’s the only motherfucker I know who could walk into a Michelin-star restaurant and still *hope* they have roasted broccoli on the menu.”**  

Tim **laughed.**  

Naomi **giggled.**  

Jodi **squared her shoulders, preparing for battle.**  

**“Alright. Let’s go find out if I have a goddamn chair.”**  

Because if she didn’t?  

**Jeff was getting a *very* public lap dance.**  

---

### **A CHAIR FOR POLISHED ICE & A RETURN TO WORK**  
Jodi **strode into the dining area and immediately started counting.**  

Five chairs for the band. **Check.**  

And—**a sixth.**  

Jodi **exhaled in satisfaction.**  

**Madeline was allowed to live.**  

The **room smelled incredible.**  

Like **a bakery, but richer, deeper—**the kind of smell that made your stomach ache with hunger before you even saw the food.  

And speaking of food—  

That **maniac little girl chef** was behind the counter, **wielding a knife bigger than her goddamn arm,** slicing roast beef into **perfect, manageable portions** with **surgical precision.**  

Jodi **grinned.**  

This **catered lunch crap?**  

**The absolute *bomb.***  

Naomi, **grabbing a plate, smirked.** **"So, think Cremeans is gonna open with another prayer?"**  

Tim, **chuckling, shook his head.** **"Nah. That’s only a morning thing."**  

Jodi **raised an eyebrow.** **"And everyone just… goes along with it?"**  

Tim **shrugged.** **"Most people humor him. But it does *ground* them each day. And the band loves the guy."**  

Jodi, **picking up a roll, frowned slightly.**  

**“First time he’s really been back to work in two years, huh?”**  

Tim **nodded.** **“Yeah. Since his wife passed.”**  

Jodi **sighed.**  

**Breast cancer.**  

She remembered when it happened. **It had wrecked him.**  

And now?  

Now he was **back.**  

Still the same **steady presence.** Still the same **rock for the band.**  

Jodi, **quiet for a moment, then muttered—**  

**“Good to see him back in it.”**  

Tim **nodded.** **"Yeah. It really is."**  

---

### **LUNCH, SWEET TEA, AND PEOPLE-WATCHING**  

Jodi **moved through the line, eyes scanning the options.**  

Sandwich? **Check.**  

Side? **Check.**  

And then—**an iced tea.**  

She hesitated, giving the **tiny terror of a chef** a skeptical look.  

**“This isn’t some weak-ass English tea, is it?”**  

The chef, **clearly offended by the very *idea***, squared her tiny shoulders and said, **“It is properly American. I *did my research*.”**  

Jodi, **grinning, picked up the glass.**  

**“Good kid.”**  

She took a **sip.**  

And yeah—**damn. It was actually *right.***  

**Sweet. Cold. Perfect.**  

Jodi made a mental note: **this kid was going places.**  

---

### **SITTING NEXT TO JEFF & THE ANIMATED BULLSHIT**  

She found her **spot at the big boys’ table, right next to Jeff.**  

Madeline was **allowed to keep her job.**  

Jodi, **finally seated, finally settled,** indulged in a bit of **people-watching.**  

Jeff was **deep in conversation with the band, hands moving animatedly, eyes lit up.**  

Whatever they were talking about—**some recording technique, some mix, some nerdy musician bullshit—**he was **fully in his element.**  

Jodi **chewed her sandwich, half-listening, half-amused.**  

She loved seeing Jeff like this. **Unfiltered. Engaged. Laughing.**  

It was one of those moments where she remembered—**oh yeah. This is why he’s great.**  

Jodi took another sip of her tea, smirking slightly.  

**This was good.**  

For the first time in… **what felt like days**—  

She was **warm. Fed. And surrounded by the only brand of insanity she actually enjoyed.**  

---

### **TAKING STOCK OF THE TABLE**  

Jodi, **casually sipping her sweet tea, let her gaze drift across the table, quietly taking stock of everyone.**  

#### **Jim: The Ragged Machine**  
Still **not shaved.** Still **running himself into the ground.**  

But his **cheeks were as ruddy as ever**, so at least he wasn’t on the verge of collapse.  

**Yet.**  

Jodi made a mental note: **if Jim ever looked *pale*, that’s when they’d need to start worrying.**  

#### **Jeremy: Holding the Line**  
Jeremy was **the only other one at the table without a beer.**  

Committed to **sobriety.**  

And, to Jodi’s quiet relief, **he seemed comfortable.**  

No tension in his shoulders. No awkward **“I swear I’m fine”** energy.  

Just **relaxed, eating his sandwich, chatting with the guys.**  

**Good.**  

He was **handling it.**  

#### **Bill: The Mystery Night Owl**  
Bill’s **hair was getting *long*.**  

Like, **80s hair-metal long.**  

The waves had started **falling into his face**, and Jodi, watching him now, noticed something else—  

**He looked *wrecked.* Exhausted.**  

**How late was he staying up alone in the studio?**  

Jodi made **another mental note.**  

Someone needed to figure out **how much sleep Bill was *not* getting.**  

#### **Avril: Suspiciously Serene**  
And then there was **Avril.**  

Mellow. **Serene. Even-keeled.**  

So fucking **calm** that it was *almost* unsettling.  

Jodi, **still fundamentally incapable of trusting Avril’s existence,** squinted slightly at her.  

And yet—  

When Jodi reached for the **salt shaker**, Avril **gently passed it over, even smiling slightly.**  

A **gentle smile.**  

Like some **enlightened sage who had just achieved inner peace.**  

Jodi, **accepting the shaker, muttered a quiet—**  

**“…Thanks.”**  

Avril **just nodded.**  

Jodi, **pouring salt onto her food, frowned slightly.**  

This **medicated-ass bitch was *so* mellow.**  

Jodi didn’t **like it.**  

At all.  

---

### **STORYTIME WITH POLISHED ICE**  

Avril, **still looking suspiciously serene, still unsettlingly mellow,** suddenly turned to Jodi and, in the same calm voice, asked—  

**“So… what was that helicopter ride like?”**  

Jodi **paused, mid-bite.**  

She **hadn’t been expecting that.**  

And yet—  

When she glanced around the table, she saw **all eyes suddenly on her.**  

The guys looked **interested.**  

Even Jeff, who had been **deep in some nerdy music conversation, turned toward her.**  

**“Yeah,”** he said, **grinning slightly.** **“We haven’t even had time for you to unleash your tale.”**  

Jodi **exhaled slowly, trying to decide where to even *start*.**  

Then—  

Jim, **smirking, took a sip of his beer, then muttered—**  

**“Damn, Jeff. Thought you said you didn’t get laid last night.”**  

The entire table **burst out laughing.**  

Jodi, **snorting, nearly choked on her tea.**  

Jeff, **rolling his eyes, smirked.** **“You *wish* I had an excuse. Nah, man. I just haven’t had time to hear the bullshit she got up to.”**  

Jodi **wiped her mouth, still grinning.**  

Fine.  

If they wanted a **story?**  

She’d **give them one.**  

She **set her drink down, stretched her arms—winced, because fuck, she was *still sore as hell*—and sighed dramatically.**  

**“Alright, assholes. You want the *truth* about my night?”**  

The guys **leaned in.**  

Jodi **grinned.**  

**“Buckle the fuck up.”**  

---

### **THE BALLAD OF POLISHED ICE**  

Jodi **settled in, smirking, savoring the moment.**  

She had **the benefit of telling the absolute truth.**  

No embellishment necessary. **The reality was already insane enough.**  

She took a **deep breath, exhaled, and then—**  

She **launched in.**  

---

#### **THE EXTRACTION: "THEY FUCKING RAPPELLED OUT OF THE SKY FOR ME."**  

**“So. There I was. Minding my own fucking business, halfway through a normal goddamn vacation, when—”**  

She slapped a hand on the table.  

**“FOUR NORWEGIAN ARMY VIKINGS SCREAM OUT OF THE ARCTIC NIGHT.”**  

Bill **raised an eyebrow.** **“Four?”**  

Jodi **grinned.** **“*Four.*”**  

Naomi, **smirking, sipped her drink.** **“God, I love this story already.”**  

**“These motherfuckers deploy *smoke*, come in *hot*, and before I know it, they are *rappelling out of the sky like a goddamn Tom Clancy novel.*”**  

Jim **chuckled, shaking his head.**  

Avril, **genuinely intrigued, muttered—** **“Jesus.”**  

**“Then comes Løytnant Tandstad—**” Jodi gestured vaguely, **“—blonde, lethal, *deeply* unbothered by committing kidnapping.”**  

Jeff **snorted.**  

**“I don’t even get a *hello* before I’m getting *hauled onto a helicopter* like an *actual fugitive.*”**  

Jeremy **grinned.** **“They at least ask nicely?”**  

**“No, Jeremy. They did *not* ask nicely. They threw me on a fucking aircraft, strapped me in, and *some asshole took a picture of me grabbing my own tits mid-flight.*”**  

Jim **nearly spit out his beer.**  

Bill, **already wheezing, choked out—** **“Wait. *What?*”**  

Jodi **pointed at him.** **“Oh yeah. That *legendary* photo? You know the one.”**  

Tim, **grinning like a bastard, leaned back.** **“Projected it *two stories tall* on the wall.”**  

Jeff, **laughing into his drink.** **“I *heard* about that.”**  

Jodi **threw her hands up.** **“IT WAS TAKEN FROM A FUCKING F-35.”**  

Silence.  

Then?  

Jim, **stunned, finally managed—** **“…They deployed a *fighter jet* to take a *boob shot?***”  

Jodi, **dead serious—** **“Yup.”**  

The entire table **collapsed into laughter.**  

---

#### **THE HELICOPTER RIDE: “FUN MANEUVER! PROBABLY WON’T HIT A MOUNTAIN!”**  

Jodi, **grinning wide now, let them settle before continuing.**  

**“So. We’re *barreling* through the Arctic at *130 knots*, dodging mountains, flying *two hundred feet* above the ground, *total darkness.*”**  

Jeremy **winced.** **“Fuck *that.*”**  

**“And then the co-pilot *casually* tells me that if I puke, they’ll just *tilt the chopper* so I can aim for the ocean.”**  

Bill **laughed.** **“Very *thoughtful* of them.”**  

Jodi **smirked.** **“I didn’t puke. Which, apparently, made me an *instant legend*.”**  

Tim **grinned.** **“Norwegians respect a bitch who can hold her liquor and her stomach.”**  

Jodi **snorted.** **“Yeah, well. They named me *Polished Ice* right then and there.”**  

Avril, **sipping her drink, tilted her head.** **“Polished Ice, huh?”**  

Jodi **sighed, shaking her head.** **“I have *no escape.*”**  

---

#### **THE "DEBRIEF" THAT WASN’T: "DRINK, POLISHED ICE!"**  

**“So I land at the base, assuming I’m about to get questioned, right? Formal debriefing? Official shit?”**  

She pointed at the table.  

**“*Nope.* I get *marched* into a bar *with two hundred screaming soldiers.*”**  

Jeff **laughed.** **“They threw you *right* in, huh?”**  

**“Oh yeah. The whole room *erupted.* Chants. Barking. Some dude in the corner just straight-up *howling.*”**  

Jim **grinned.** **“And you?”**  

Jodi **sighed, gesturing.** **“Then the general walks in. *Barks.* And the whole fucking unit barks *back.*”**  

Bill **was *losing* it.** **“No *way.*”**  

Jodi **grinned.** **“And then the general challenges me to a drinking contest.”**  

Tim, **shaking his head.** **“Like I said—*instant legend.*”**  

---

#### **THE AFTERMATH: "ONE OF US! ONE OF US!"**  

Jodi, **sipping her tea dramatically, sighed.**  

**“I hold my own. I survive. I drink *nine beers* in two and a half hours. I don’t puke. I don’t shit myself. *I make America proud.*”**  

Jeremy **winced.** **“How the fuck did you not die?”**  

**“*Sheer fucking willpower.*”**  

Avril, **grinning slightly.** **“And then?”**  

Jodi **sighed.**  

**“Then I nearly *died* trying to find the bathroom, got pranked by my *own fucking escort officer*, and then got dragged *right back to the bar* for more.”**  

Jim **laughed.** **“And now you’re *one of them.*”**  

Jodi **nodded solemnly.**  

**“That’s what they kept chanting. *One of us! One of us!*”**  

Bill, **grinning, lifted his beer.** **“Well, shit. Here’s to *Polished Ice.*”**  

Everyone at the table **raised their glasses.**  

Jodi, **grinning despite herself, clinked her tea against Jeff’s beer and exhaled.**  

**“God *damn* it, Norway.”**  

---

### **DIPLOMATIC ACHIEVEMENTS & CANADIAN RESISTANCE**  

Jeff, **grinning, took a sip of his beer and smirked at Jodi.**  

**“Babe, you’ve probably done more for U.S.-Norwegian relations than anyone else in ages.”**  

Jodi, **rolling her eyes, sighed.**  

**“Great. Where’s my goddamn *medal?***”  

Avril, **raising a finger, smirking slightly—**  

**“Don’t forget about the *Great White North!*”**  

Bill, **without missing a beat, turned to her.**  

**“Yeah, yeah, Avril. When are you finally moving to Florida like the rest of your goddamn country?”**  

The table **cracked up.**  

Avril, **grinning, shook her head.** **“Bitch, *never.*”**  

Bill, **grinning back, waggled his beer at her.** **“You *say* that now, but eventually, you’re gonna give in.”**  

Jodi, **chuckling, leaned back.** **“He’s not wrong. It’s only a matter of time before you’re in a *gated community* with a *pink flamingo lawn ornament.*”**  

Avril **rolled her eyes, but she was still smirking.** **“I *refuse.*”**  

Tim, **grinning, chimed in.**  

**“You say that now, but wait ‘til you hit fifty and suddenly *taxes* start to matter.”**  

Avril, **laughing, shook her head.**  

**“I’ll take my chances, thanks.”**  

Jodi, **deadpan, took another sip of her tea.**  

**“Yeah. That’s what *every* Canadian says. Right before they end up in *Tampa.*”**  

---
### **FAKING NICE & THE ALIEN QUEEN**  

Avril **giggled like a little schoolgirl.**  

And that? **That right there was unsettling as fuck.**  

Jodi **stared at her, utterly perplexed.**  

**Why the hell was she *afraid* of this woman?**  

She wasn’t **threatening.** She wasn’t **loud.**  

She was **serene, polite, and somehow… *giggling*.**  

Jodi’s stomach **twisted.**  

Then, out of the corner of her eye, she **caught Jeff watching her.**  

**Sizing her up.**  

And worst of all? **Beaming.**  

And **just like that?**  

Jodi **remembered *exactly* why she hated Avril.**  

That little look on Jeff’s face? **That smug, knowing, “she’s growing on you” bullshit?**  

**Oh, fuck *off.***  

Jodi, **hiding every ounce of irritation, took a slow breath.**  

She could do this.  

She could be **nice.**  

She could be **charming.**  

She could be **the sweet, sociable, ever-lovable Jodi.**  

She would **pretend her ass off for the rest of this trip.**  

She would **not**—**under any circumstances—**emulate **Sigourney Weaver in *Aliens*.**  

She would **not** look at Avril and see a **horrifying extraterrestrial horror-bitch queen nesting in Jeff’s brain.**  

She would **not** mentally prepare to wield a flamethrower.  

She would **not.**  

Jodi **exhaled, steeled herself, and put on her absolute best, award-winning, “I am perfectly pleasant” smile.**  

And said, in the **most convincing voice she could muster—**  

**“Avril, babe, I *love* your energy today.”**  

Avril **beamed.**  

Jeff **grinned knowingly.**  

And Jodi?  

Jodi just **prayed for strength.**

---

### **THE COMING BROCCOLI APOCALYPSE**  

Jodi **had eaten roasted broccoli before.**  

She wasn’t **immune** to its charms.  

She could even **admit** that it was **decent.**  

But right now?  

She wasn’t thinking about the **flavor.**  

She wasn’t thinking about the **nutritional benefits.**  

She was thinking about **five PM.**  

**When these same two dozen people…**  

Would be **crammed into a very small section…**  

Of a **very small recording studio…**  

**And start *farting*.**  

Jodi’s **fork paused mid-air.**  

Her stomach **sank.**  

She **glanced around the table.**  

Everyone was **happily eating.** **No concerns. No hesitation.**  

Even Jeff, the **number-one broccoli enthusiast on planet Earth,** was **mowing through his plate with zero fear.**  

Jodi, **mouth tightening, exhaled slowly.**  

**They had no idea what they were about to unleash.**  

And worst of all?  

**They’d be trapped in a sealed, soundproofed room.**  

No **ventilation.**  

No **escape.**  

Jodi slowly turned to Naomi, her voice **grim, foreboding.**  

**“…This is gonna be *so* bad later.”**  

Naomi, **blinking, frowned.** **“What?”**  

Jodi, **lowering her voice like she was about to deliver the **darkest** prophecy of all time—**  

**“The broccoli, Naomi. The *broccoli.*”**  

Naomi **froze.**  

Then, **slowly, realization dawned.**  

Her **eyes widened slightly.**  

She looked at her plate. Then at Jodi.  

Then at the **tiny, crowded, inescapable recording studio waiting for them.**  

**“…Oh. *Oh.*”**  

Jodi **just nodded.**  

And across the table?  

Jeff, **completely oblivious, grinned and popped another forkful into his mouth.**  

**Happy. Carefree. Unaware that he had just personally ensured the studio’s suffering.**  

Jodi just **prayed she wouldn’t suffocate before the album was finished.**  

---

### **NAOMI, THE VOICE OF REASON (FOR ONCE)**  

Naomi, **blissfully detached from the nightmare scenario Jodi was envisioning,** tilted her head and asked—  

**“Can’t we just… go do something else then?”**  

Jodi **blinked.** **“What?”**  

Naomi **shrugged.** **“Like, take a train ride? Watch a hockey game downtown? Do you know how to ice skate?”**  

Jodi **stared.**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“I *know* they have a skating rink for residents.”**  

Jodi **continued staring.**  

Because—**holy shit.**  

That was **so simple.**  

So **logical.**  

So **utterly removed** from the **suffocating doom** that awaited them in the studio.  

And yet?  

Jodi **hadn’t even considered it.**  

Tim, **grinning, glanced at Jodi.** **“Babe, your brain just short-circuited.”**  

Jodi, **still processing, slowly muttered—**  

**“…Naomi, are you telling me we don’t *have* to spend our afternoon in a *gassy death chamber*?”**  

Naomi **rolled her eyes.** **“Babe, we’re in *Norway*. There are, like, *other things to do.*”**  

Jodi, **exhaling, leaning back in her chair, dramatically declared—**  

**“You may have just *saved my life*.”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“I do what I can.”**  

Tim, **smirking, sipped his drink.** **“So, Jodi. What’s it gonna be? Studio *or* skating?”**  

Jodi, **without hesitation—**  

**“*Fuck* the studio. I’m getting on a train.”**  

---

### **THE ESCAPE FROM BROCCOLI DOOM**  

Madeline, **ever-efficient, ever in control, pulled up to the train station, put the car in park, and turned to Jodi and Naomi with her usual level of deadly competence.**  

**“Text me thirty minutes before you’re heading back so I can arrange your ride to the hotel.”**  

Jodi **nodded.** **“Got it, boss.”**  

Madeline **gave them both a sharp, approving look before driving off, leaving them on their own.**  

Naomi, **hands in her coat pockets, looked around.** **“Alright, Jodes. Where to?”**  

Jodi, **adjusting her bag strap, thought about it.**  

**Where *did* she want to go?**  

Somewhere **calm.** Somewhere **quiet.**  

Somewhere that **didn’t involve a sealed room filled with broccoli-fueled biological warfare.**  

She exhaled, watching her breath fog in the cold air.  

**“Around the town and back.”**  

Naomi **raised an eyebrow.** **“That’s it?”**  

Jodi **shrugged.** **“Didn’t get to see much of the countryside while flying yesterday. Was a little busy trying *not* to puke or die.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Reasonable.”**  

Jodi **sighed, tilting her head, watching a train approach in the distance.**  

**“A nice, *sedate* train ride around the area? No chaos? No helicopters? No screaming lunatics? That sounds *perfect*.”**  

Naomi **grinned, nudging her.** **“Babe, let’s be real. If anyone on this train so much as sneezes too loud, *your* ass will be at the center of some bullshit by the end of the ride.”**  

Jodi, **deadpan, turned to her.**  

**“…I *fucking* hope not.”**  

Naomi **just laughed, linking arms with Jodi as they walked toward the platform.**  

The train **pulled in, doors sliding open.**  

And for the first time in **what felt like days—**  

Jodi was **finally going to get some goddamn *peace*.**  

Probably.

---

### **A QUIET TOUR OF NOWHERE**  

Jodi and Naomi **settled into their seats**, the train **humming softly as it pulled away from the station.**  

For the first time in what felt like **forever**, Jodi wasn’t **running, drinking, or actively trying to survive the people around her.**  

Just **a quiet ride.**  

A chance to **breathe.**  

And as they rode around the **perimeter of the city**, Jodi took it all in.  

It was… **smaller than she expected.**  

Compact. **Efficient.**  

The harbor? **Bleak.**  

The sea? **Even bleaker.**  

Grey, **restless, cold as hell.**  

Jodi, **watching the waves churn against the docks, exhaled slowly.** **“God, I hope this place looks nicer in the summer.”**  

Naomi **chuckled, leaning her head against the window.** **“Babe, you came to the Arctic in *January.* What *were* you expecting?”**  

Jodi **shrugged.** **“Less *post-apocalyptic*?”**  

Naomi **snorted.**  

But the mountains?  

The mountains were **gorgeous.**  

Towering, **snow-drenched, jagged against the grey sky.**  

And the train tunnels—**carved deep into them—felt *ancient*.**  

Like they had been **chiseled out of the earth in the 1800s**, **long before machines, before efficiency, before anything but sheer stubborn human will.**  

Jodi **traced a finger along the frost on the window, watching as the darkness of another tunnel swallowed them.**  

For all the **chaos** this trip had thrown at her, at least this?  

This was **peaceful.**  

Quiet.  

A chance to just **exist.**  

She could live with that.

---

### **THE INEVITABLE RECOGNITION**  

Jodi, **gazing out the window, tracing idle shapes in the frost, suddenly felt… watched.**  

She **shifted, just enough to glance to her left without making it obvious.**  

Up and to the side, a woman sat **alone, occasionally sneaking looks in their direction.**  

Jodi **exhaled through her nose.**  

**“…There’s some chick up to our left checking me out.”**  

Naomi, **grinning immediately, perked up.**  

**“Like she wants to *bang*?”**  

Jodi **rolled her eyes.** **“Probably not.”**  

She glanced at the woman again.  

There was a **hesitation** in the way she looked, like she was **debating whether or not to say something.**  

Jodi sighed.  

**“She’s probably seen me on the *freaking internet*.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Babe, you *did* get extracted by the Norwegian military *on camera*. You’re basically a cryptid now.”**  

Jodi **grumbled.** **“A cryptid wouldn’t have to deal with small talk.”**  

They **waited**, but the woman **didn’t approach.**  

Jodi wondered if she ever **would.**  

But for now?  

The ride **continued.**  

Stop after stop, the train **moved through the landscape.**  

And god—**this place looked so different than Northwest Ohio.**  

The buildings, the streets, the mountains in the distance—**it was a completely different world.**  

Cold, stark, and **so damn foreign** to everything Jodi had grown up around.  

She wasn’t **sure if she loved it yet.**  

But at least?  

It was **interesting.**  

---

### **RELAXING OR STEWING?**  

Naomi, **leaning her head against the window, watching the mountains blur past, suddenly frowned.**  

**“…Babe.”**  

Jodi, **still gazing out at the landscape, humming absently, barely reacted.**  

**“Hmm?”**  

Naomi **tilted her head, thoughtful.**  

**“We’ve been riding around for, like… two hours.”**  

Jodi **blinked, then checked her watch.**  

**Oh.**  

Yeah. That tracked.  

Naomi, **eyebrows raised, studied her.**  

**“So. Are you *relaxing*… or *stewing*?”**  

Jodi **sighed deeply, tapping her fingers against her thigh.**  

**Good question.**  

She **didn’t even know the answer.**  

She wasn’t **actively angry.** Not **anxious.**  

But was she **actually enjoying this?**  

Or just **letting her brain spiral in a quiet, scenic setting?**  

She finally glanced at Naomi, **expression unreadable.**  

**“…Yes.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Goddamn it, Jodi.”**  

Jodi **grinned slightly, then sighed, looking back out the window.**  

**“…I think I’m doing both.”**  

Naomi **chuckled.** **“Yeah. That sounds right.”**  

---

### **AVRIL, JEFF’S DICK, AND HARDER DRUGS**  

Naomi, **watching Jodi carefully, smirked.**  

**“So, be real with me. Is this all about *Avril* and Jeff’s *dick*?”**  

Jodi **exhaled sharply, shaking her head.**  

**“Jesus *Christ*, Naomi.”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“I mean, that *is* what you’re stewing about, right?”**  

Jodi **didn’t answer immediately.**  

Because—**fuck.**  

She *wasn’t* actually sure.  

It wasn’t just **Avril.**  

And it wasn’t just **Jeff.**  

But the combination of those two things? **Yeah. That wasn’t helping.**  

Before she could respond, Naomi, **ever the agent of chaos, continued—**  

**“Maybe next time I should pop MDMA with Avril. Really get to know her.”**  

Jodi **whipped her head around.** **“The *fuck* you will.”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“What? I’m *curious*.”**  

Jodi **glared.** **“Yeah? Well, *be curious* about literally *anything else.*”**  

Naomi **grinned wider.** **“Come on, Jodes. You don’t want me to get all mellow and *serene* like Avril?”**  

Jodi **gave her the most deadpan look possible.**  

**“…If you *ever* start giggling like a schoolgirl, I’m throwing you off this train.”**  

Naomi **laughed harder.** **“Duly noted.”**  

Jodi, **grumbling, crossed her arms and stared back out the window.**  

She was **not ready for a world where Naomi got *weirdly nice, too*.**

---

### **CONVERTING FREEDOM UNITS**  

Naomi, **already pulling out her phone, casually said—**  

**“Texting Madeline. We’ve got two stops and forty-six kilometers left, according to the display.”**  

Jodi, **frowning slightly, turned to her.**  

**“How much is that distance in *American*?”**  

Naomi **snorted.**  

**“Jesus, Jodi.”**  

Jodi **shrugged.** **“Look, I don’t *speak* the metric system.”**  

Naomi, **already tapping into Google, muttered,** **“You *could* learn, you know.”**  

Jodi **raised an eyebrow.** **“Or I could just *not*.”**  

Naomi **sighed dramatically, then read off her screen—**  

**“It’s about… twenty-eight and a half miles.”**  

Jodi **nodded approvingly.**  

**“Ah. A *real* measurement.”**  

Naomi **rolled her eyes, texting Madeline.**  

**“You are *so* American it *hurts.*”**  

Jodi **grinned, stretching.**  

**“Yeah. And *proud of it.*”**  

---

### **STEAM ROOMS & CRIMINAL TRENDS**  

Naomi, **still texting, still smirking, glanced up.**  

**“So, are you finally gonna join me tonight and soak in the heat?”**  

Jodi, **raising an eyebrow, leaned back.**  

**“Mmm. Tempting.”**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“Babe, so far, I’ve had the *weirdest* shit happen in that steam room.”**  

Jodi, **tilting her head, intrigued despite herself.**  

**“Yeah? Like what?”**  

Naomi **counted off on her fingers.**  

**“One, a *very* enlightening talk about MDMA with Avril.”**  

Jodi **groaned.** **“Fucking Avril.”**  

**“Two, some dude with the *thickest* accent I’ve ever heard casually admitted to *major* tax fraud.”**  

Jodi **perked up.** **“Okay, *now* we’re talking.”**  

Naomi, **grinning, leaned in.**  

**“So, if I go tonight… what are the *odds* of a trifecta of *criminal behavior*?”**  

Jodi, **smirking, pretended to think deeply.**  

**“Well. Based on current data? We’ve got drug talk, financial crime… logically, the next one should be *violent.*”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“Babe, I swear to God, if someone confesses to *murder* tonight, I’m *never* leaving the steam room again.”**  

Jodi **grinned.**  

**“Alright, fuck it. I’ll go. But if this turns into some *weird-ass* confessional, you’re buying me a drink after.”**  

Naomi **beamed.**  

**“Deal. Now let’s go see if the hotel’s still standing.”**

### **THE UNFORTUNATE TALLY OF NAKEDNESS**  

Naomi, **grinning as she tucked her phone away, added one last thing—**  

**“Oh, and if Bill’s in the steam room tonight? Definitely *don’t* stare at his plum-sized balls, or he’ll take it as an *invitation.*”**  

Jodi **froze mid-step.**  

**“…I *beg* your fucking pardon?”**  

Naomi, **completely unfazed.** **“Oh yeah. He’s *very* comfortable. And if he catches you looking, well… he’ll assume you *want* to look.”**  

Jodi **dragged a hand down her face.**  

**“Jesus. *Noted.*”**  

Then, after a beat, she turned to Naomi with a **deeply suspicious** look.  

**“Okay. *Important question.*”**  

Naomi **raised an eyebrow.**  

Jodi **crossed her arms.**  

**“How many people have you seen *naked* so far on this trip?”**  

Naomi, **without hesitation, started counting on her fingers.**  

**“Bill, obviously. Tim. Avril, for a bit in the sauna. Some random Norwegian dude. And… I *think* I saw a sliver of Jeff’s ass one morning, but I was only half awake, so that might not count.”**  

Jodi **stared at her.**  

Naomi **grinned.**  

Jodi, **exhaling slowly, shook her head.**  

**“…What *the fuck* is this trip?”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“A goddamn *blessing*.”**  

---

### **THE ROMANCE DEFICIT & THE STEAM ROOM SOLUTION**  

Jodi **sighed, shaking her head as the train slowed toward their stop.**  

**“Okay. Fine. I’ll admit it.”**  

Naomi, **perking up, grinning.** **“Oh? Admitting what?”**  

Jodi **rolled her eyes.**  

**“I’m having a *blast* on this trip.”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“Uh-huh. But?”**  

Jodi **exhaled, rubbing her temples.**  

**“But it’s been a *lot* less romance and sex with Jeff than I anticipated.”**  

Naomi **smirked.** **“A tragedy.”**  

Jodi **shrugged.** **“The sleigh rides are *great*, but they’re a *commute.* I *loved* the acoustics in the hotel room and the fact that *everyone* heard exactly how much Jeff loves me—”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Oh, *everyone* knows, babe.”**  

**“—but somehow, my biggest fun thing on this trip was a *death ride* with a bunch of Viking warriors *led by a painfully thin blonde.*”**  

Naomi **laughed harder.**  

Jodi **sighed dramatically, stretching.**  

**“Maybe soaking in the sauna will purge the last bit of alcohol from my system.”**  

Naomi **raised an eyebrow.** **“Oh? We’re calling it a *detox* now?”**  

Jodi, **deadpan, shrugged.**  

**“Maybe there’s *something* to this woo-woo bullshit after all.”**  

Naomi, **grinning, hooked her arm through Jodi’s as they stepped off the train.**  

**“Babe, by the end of this trip, I *swear* I’m gonna get you into yoga.”**  

Jodi **groaned.** **“*Don’t* push your luck.”**  

---

### **STEAM ROOM TIME: DETOX OR DELUSION?**  

After finally **arriving back at the hotel**, Jodi **pushed open the door to their room and immediately noticed something.**  

Jeff **wasn’t there.**  

His **loss.**  

She **shrugged, shut the door, and didn’t even hesitate.**  

**Clothes? Gone.**  

She **stripped naked in record time, letting out a satisfied sigh as she tossed on one of those impossibly soft, high-end hotel bathrobes.**  

Seriously. **Whoever picked these out deserved a raise.**  

She **collected Naomi, who was already ready to go, equally bundled up in a robe.**  

Naomi **grinned.** **“Fully committing to this detox shit, huh?”**  

Jodi **tied her belt, rolling her shoulders.**  

**“Eh. We’ll see if it’s a *detox* or just a *really warm mistake*.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“Either way, babe. You’re about to sweat *everything* out.”**  

Jodi **sighed dramatically, opening the door.**  

**“Let’s just get this over with before Bill shows up and air-dries his balls again.”**  

Naomi, **laughing, followed her outside.**  

The cold **bit through the air as they stepped into the night.**  

The **nearby sauna was waiting.**  

And if the past few days were any indication?  

**This was *not* going to be just a normal, relaxing soak.**  

---

### **THE UNTOUCHABLE MADELINE**  

Jodi **paused mid-step**, watching as **Madeline casually approached—wearing heels.**  

On **six inches of fucking snow.**  

And not just any snow—**crisp, crunchy, deceptive shit** that should have **instantly betrayed her.**  

But somehow? **Her heels didn’t even *sink.***  

Jodi **stared.**  

That **defied physics.**  

And to make it worse?  

The woman was **wearing a dress so tight it *hugged her ass like it was custom-molded*—and yet?**  

**No panty lines.**  

Jodi, **internally sighing, thought—**  

**Oh, to be 28 again.**  

Hell, **she doubted Madeline was even *that* old.**  

Naomi, **walking beside her, grinned and called out—**  

**“Hey, question. How come no one dares to call you *Maddie*?”**  

Madeline, **not even breaking stride, smirked slightly.**  

Then, in **perfectly even, borderline terrifying calm—**  

**“Because they know better.”**  

Naomi **snorted.**  

Jodi, **grinning, whispered—**  

**“Fucking *terrifying*.”**  

Madeline **just smiled, gave them a nod, and disappeared into the hotel.**  

Leaving Jodi to **marvel once more at whatever unholy pact that woman had made with the universe.**  

---

### **THE SCARIEST RECORD EXECUTIVE: SARAH VS. MADELINE**  

Jodi, **watching Madeline disappear into the hotel like some kind of untouchable ice queen, muttered—**  

**“I honestly can’t tell who’s scarier, Sarah or Madeline.”**  

Naomi, **frowning slightly.** **“Wait—who the *hell* is Sarah?”**  

Jodi **blinked.**  

**Oops.**  

**“Oh—shit. She’s not in Norway.”**** Jodi waved a hand.** **“Sarah’s Jeff’s old record executive. *Madeline’s* her new personal assistant. And, yeah, she’s a *fucking* chip off the old block.”**  

Naomi, **intrigued, smirked.** **“And you’re not… competitive about Sarah?”**  

Jodi **snorted.** **“Not even a little. Sarah only has *eyes* for her hubby.”**  

Naomi **tilted her head.** **“That’s… kind of a rarity in the entertainment industry, huh?”**  
Jodi **shrugged.** **“Yep. But that’s just how she is.”**  

Naomi, **raising an eyebrow, grinning slightly.** **“You *do* realize Jeff also works in that very industry, right?”**  

Jodi, **deadpan, smirked.**  

**“And my point *still stands*.”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“Damn. That’s some confidence.”**  

Jodi **grinned, finally pushing open the door to the sauna.**  

**“Babe, it ain’t confidence. It’s just *facts*.”**  

---

### **THE HEAT & THE UNNERVING STILLNESS**  

Naomi, **grinning as they stepped toward the sauna, casually muttered—**  

**“I mean, Jeff seems like he’d fuck just about *anybody*.”**  

Jodi **rolled her eyes.**  

**“Jesus, Naomi.”**  

Before she could say more, her gaze **snapped forward—**  

And she **immediately stopped.**  

Because **there, in the sauna, sitting on the floor—**  

**Was Avril.**  

Head between her knees.  

Hands **resting on top of them.**  

Completely **motionless.**  

Not adjusting.  

Not shifting.  

Not even **acknowledging their presence.**  

Jodi **felt her stomach tighten.**  

Because **something about it was wrong.**  

She wasn’t just **resting.**  

She wasn’t **asleep.**  

She was **too still.**  

Almost **preternaturally still.**  

Jodi and Naomi **hung up their bathrobes, stepping into the hellacious heat.**  

And Jodi, **eyes locked on Avril, immediately thought—**  

**What the *fuck* is going on here?**

### **DINNER PLANS & THE CANADIAN STATUE**  

Jodi and Naomi **stepped fully into the sauna, the heat slamming into them like a brick wall.**  

Naomi, **already thinking ahead, sighed dramatically.** **“Alright. What do we think dinner’s gonna be tonight?”**  

Jodi, **keeping her voice casual but her eyes locked on Avril, shrugged.** **“Hopefully something *normal*. I don’t think I can survive another ‘regional delicacy’ night.”**  

Naomi **snorted.** **“No dried fish? No fermented shark?”**  

Jodi **gave her a look.** **“Babe, if they bring out *another* dish that smells like *death itself*, I’m putting in a fucking room service order for a cheeseburger.”**  

Naomi **laughed.** **“Alright, so… best-case scenario?”**  

Jodi, **still watching Avril, muttered—** **“Something hot. Something filling. Meat, potatoes, a soup, maybe?”**  

Naomi **sighed, stretching.** **“Man, I *do* want a good soup.”**  

Jodi **nodded absently.**  

Because Avril?  

**Hadn’t. Moved. Once.**  

She was **still sitting there.**  

**Still naked.**  

**Still eerily fucking *motionless.***  

Jodi, **eyebrows furrowing slightly, finally leaned over and whispered to Naomi—**  

**“…Okay. Is she asleep, or is she dead?”**  

Naomi **glanced over, raising an eyebrow.**  

Then?  

She **froze.**  

Because yeah—**that was not normal.**  

Avril was just **sitting there.**  

No sign of breathing.  

No sign of even being **aware** they’d entered.  

Naomi, **brow furrowing, whispered back—**  

**“…I dunno, babe. But I *really* don’t want to be the one to check.”**  

---

### **THE POWER PLAY THAT DIDN’T LAND**  

Jodi, **never one to back down from a challenge—even an unspoken, deeply weird one—decided to push her luck.**  

She took a **few slow steps forward**, deliberately **positioning herself directly in front of Avril.**  

If Avril **looked up, the first thing she’d see?**  

**Jodi’s twat.**  

No avoiding it. **No looking past it.**  

Avril would have to **stare down the reality** that Jeff **fucked that**—and **not her.**  

Maybe this was a **power move.**  

Maybe it was **petty as hell.**  

Either way?  

**Jodi was committing.**  

She waited.  

And then—  

Avril, **slowly, with eerie calm, finally lifted her head.**  

And instead of **shock, discomfort, or literally any reaction Jodi was expecting—**  

Avril **just smiled.**  

Soft. **Serene.**  

And in a **gentle, soothing voice,** she greeted Jodi with—  

**“Hey.”**  

Jodi **blinked.**  

Avril, **completely unfazed, continued—**  

**“I’m hoping for a cheeseburger, too.”**  

Jodi **narrowed her eyes slightly.**  

Because now?  

Now she **noticed something else.**  

Avril’s **accent.**  

It was **thicker.**  

Way more **Canadian** than when she sang, or when she was on TV.  

It was… **almost like she wasn’t trying to hide it.**  

Jodi, **staring, couldn’t stop herself from thinking—**  

**What the *fuck* is she *on*?**

### **AVRIL: HIGH, OFF-MEDS, & A WALKING PHARMACY**  

Jodi, **staring down at Avril, still way too still, way too fucking calm, finally just asked—**  

**“Are you *high*?”**  

Avril, **smiling, unfazed, replied—**  

**“I’m *complicated*.”**  

Then she **giggled.**  

Jodi **groaned.** **“Jesus *Christ*.”**  

Avril, **stretching slightly, finally shifted position, but her voice remained that same eerie, *gentle* tone.**  

**“The last couple years have been *way* too stressful, so… I’ve been on ecstasy.”**  

Jodi **blinked.** **“Like… *pharmaceutical* ecstasy?”**  

Avril **nodded.** **“Yep.”**  

**“But Norway doesn’t permit pharmaceutical use, so… I had to leave my meds at home.”**  

Jodi, **processing this, slowly asked—**  

**“…So what the *fuck* are you on right now?”**  

Avril **smiled sweetly.**  

**“I didn’t want to go without, so I’m getting pills from *Madeline*.”**  

Naomi, **who had been quietly watching this entire exchange, suddenly let out a soft—**  

**“*Oh.*”**  

Jodi, **deadpan.**  

**“Madeline.”**  

Avril **nodded, still smiling.**  

**“Madeline’s a *charming* young lass. If you guys want, she can get you some, too.”**  

Jodi, **rubbing her temples.**  

**“I *knew* that woman was a fucking *machine*, but now she’s an *international drug supplier*?”**  

Avril **giggled again.**  

Then, **completely changing the subject, she tilted her head and said—**  

**“By the way, I’m *so* envious of your deal with Rubies Bras.”**  

Jodi, **brain short-circuiting from the absolute chaos of this conversation, could only stare.**  

Naomi, **covering her mouth, whispered—**  

**“Babe, I think you *broke* her.”**  

---

### **AVRIL: HIGH, HONEST, OR BOTH?**  

Jodi, **still trying to untangle the absolute bullshit she just heard, was about to respond when—**  

Avril, **completely unbothered, casually added—**  

**“Oh, I get some from Rubies, too.”**  

Jodi **blinked.**  

Avril, **stretching her arms above her head, sighed.**  

**“I like supporting local business.”**  

Then, **with zero shame, she grabbed her own tits, juggled them a little, and declared—**  

**“Anyone with *these knockers* who *wails on a guitar* is gonna have *severe* need for proper support.”**  

Naomi, **grinning, watching this train wreck unfold, just muttered—**  

**“Facts.”**  

Avril, **nodding sagely, continued—**  

**“So, yeah. Custom-made bras? *Totally* worth it.”**  

Jodi **just stared.**  

Because now she was **debating two things.**  

**One—** Was Avril being **totally upfront and honest** because she *could* be?  

Or…  

**Two—** Was she **so baked out of her goddamn mind** that she had *no choice*?  

Jodi **rubbed her temples, exhaling slowly.**  

**“Avril, babe, I do *not* know how to handle you right now.”**  

Avril **just grinned.**  

**“Oh, that’s fine. *Most people don’t.*”**
