### **THE TRUTH SERUM OF AVRIL LAVIGNE**  

Jodi, **mind still reeling, still trying to process the absolute nonsense Avril was spilling, decided—fuck it.**  

She was **gonna push.**  

So she **tilted her head, voice casual as anything, and asked—**  

**“Why’d you get divorced the second time?”**  

Avril, **without hesitation, without even a *flicker* of hesitation—**  

**“Because of Jeff.”**  

Naomi **visibly flinched.**  

Jodi **went still.**  

Then, **slowly, evenly—**  

**“…The fuck does that mean?”**  

Avril **blinked once, then answered like it was the most normal thing in the world.**  

**“Because he needed it.”**  

Jodi’s **stomach curled.**  

Her voice, **tight.**  

**“Did you know he was *seeing me* at the time?”**  

Avril **smiled.**  

**“Yep.”**  

Jodi **felt her pulse spike.**  

**“And?”**  

Avril **shrugged.**  

**“Didn’t care.”**  

Naomi, **who had been watching this unfold with increasing alarm, suddenly had a realization.**  

And that realization was **fucking terrifying.**  

She inhaled sharply and **turned to Jodi, eyes wide.**  

**“Oh *shit*.”**  

Jodi, **still locked on Avril, muttered—**  

**“What?”**  

Naomi, **horrified.**  

**“She *can’t lie.*”**  

Jodi’s **stomach dropped.**  

Naomi, **now seriously debating whether she needed to dial Jodi back or get her *the fuck* out of here before Avril revealed *one too many truths*, muttered—**  

**“Babe, we need to leave. *Now.*”**  

Jodi, **jaw tightening, just stared at Avril, whose expression was still soft, still calm, still completely unbothered.**  

And the worst part?  

She wasn’t **fucking lying.**

---

### **THE UNFILTERED TRUTH—AND A DRUG OFFERING**  

Jodi, **voice low, testing, dangerous—**  

**“…Hold on.”**  

Avril, **serene as ever, just watched her.**  

Jodi, **eyes narrowing.**  

**“Do you like sucking his dick?”**  

Avril, **without a single pause, replied—**  

**“Every time, it’s great.”**  

Naomi **exhaled through her nose, sharp, tense.**  

Jodi, **jaw tightening.**  

**“When was the *last time*?”**  

Avril, **tilting her head, considering.**  

**“Probably ten years ago.”**  

Naomi **closed her eyes for a second, muttering,** **“Thank *fuck*.”**  

Jodi, **ignoring Naomi, pressed forward.**  

**“When was the *last time you fucked?***”  

Avril, **without hesitation, still calm as ever—**  

**“After he had an existential crisis one night and you didn’t answer the phone, so he came to my hotel room and I rode him.”**  

Naomi’s **eyes flew open.**  

Jodi, **stomach twisting, heartbeat spiking—**  

**“*What.*”**  

Avril, **exhaling softly, almost wistful—**  

**“He needed it.”**  

Naomi, **staring at Avril like she had just walked out of the goddamn void, whispered—**  

**“Jesus *Christ*.”**  

Jodi, **face unreadable, locked on Avril.**  

**“Do you still wanna fuck him?”**  

Avril, **groaning, rolling her head back, exasperated.**  

**“God, *yes.* In the *worst* way.”**  

Naomi **inhaled sharply.**  

Avril, **still eerily calm, added—**  

**“But he’s devoted to *you* and his little menagerie. And it *sucks* that I can’t get through the bedroom door.”**  

Jodi, **still not looking away, voice ice-cold.**  

**“Yeah. *It does.*”**  

Avril, **sighing, shifting slightly, then looked up again—**  

**“Are you *sure* you don’t want Madeline to get you a dose?”**  

Jodi **stiffened.**  

Naomi, **immediately tensing.**  

Avril, **smiling softly, voice soothing, unnerving—**  

**“The clarity and spirituality afterward is *really* great. And the world will just… overflow with *love*.”**  

Naomi, **without even thinking, grabbed Jodi’s wrist.**  

**“Babe. We’re leaving. *Now.*”**  

Because this?  

This was getting **too fucking deep.**

---

### **AVRIL’S PARTING WORDS & A HASTY EXIT**  

As Jodi and Naomi **began backing toward the door, pulse rates through the roof, Avril—still naked, still eerily serene—spoke one last time.**  

**“I’ll be listening for you later tonight.”**  

Jodi **froze.**  

Naomi’s **grip on her wrist *tightened*.**  

Avril, **smiling softly, continued—**  

**“But… please accept that I *wish* I was the one in bed with Jeff.”**  

Jodi’s **stomach *plummeted*.**  

Naomi **made a strangled noise.**  

Avril, **completely unbothered, added—**  

**“And I *do* hope we can all enjoy breakfast together in the morning.”**  

Jodi **didn’t respond.**  

She **turned.**  

And with **urgent, nearly frantic energy, she and Naomi skedaddled the *fuck* out of the sauna.**  

**Fast.**  

**Hurried.**  

Moving like the **devil himself was licking at their heels.**  

Because Jesus **fucking** Christ.  

That had been **too much.**

---

### **POST-AVRIL DAMAGE CONTROL: STRAIGHT TO THE BAR**  

Jodi **marched Naomi straight to the bar.**  

**Do not pass go.**  

**Do not collect $200.**  

Just **get to the goddamn alcohol.**  

Anyone who **so much as looked at them funny** for showing up in their **bathrobes?**  

**Would get bitchslapped into another dimension.**  

They hit the bar, and Jodi **slammed her hands down on the counter.**  

**“Two whiskey doubles. And waters.”**  

The bartender, **blinking at their robe-clad, slightly manic appearances,** didn’t say a word.  

Just **poured.**  

Naomi, **still looking a little dazed, finally exhaled.**  

**“Babe. What the *fuck* just happened.”**  

Jodi **grabbed her whiskey, downed half in one go, then wiped her mouth.**  

**“We *barely* escaped a cult recruitment.”**  

Naomi **snorted, shaking her head, grabbing her own glass.**  

**“Bitch really just told you she’s gonna *listen* to you fuck Jeff later.”**  

Jodi **groaned, knocking back the rest of her drink.**  

**“Oh, I *heard*.”**  

Naomi **grinned, raising her glass.**  

**“To *batshit honesty.*”**  

Jodi **clinked.**  

**“To *never doing MDMA with Avril.*”**  

And then?  

They **drank.**

---

### **BILL CALLS BULLSHIT**  

Bill **wandered over, immediately noticing their energy was *off*.**  

Not just **"weird sauna" off.**  

**Something happened.**  

He pulled up a chair, eyed their half-empty whiskey glasses, and finally asked—  

**“Alright. What the fuck did Avril do?”**  

Jodi and Naomi **both exhaled hard.**  

Then?  

They **explained.**  

The **unnerving stillness.**  

The **MDMA revelation.**  

The **Jeff confession.**  

The **fucking "I’ll be listening for you later tonight" line.**  

By the time they finished, Bill **just sighed, rubbing his face.**  

**“Yeah. Not surprised.”**  

Jodi, **narrowing her eyes.** **“Wait. *You noticed?*”**  

Bill **nodded.** **“A week ago.”**  

Naomi **blinked.** **“And you just… *let that shit ride?*”**  

Bill, **arms crossed, sighed again.**  

**“Look. She was coping *fine* for the last three months. But whatever she’s doing *now*? Yeah. It’s too much.”**  

Jodi, **jaw clenching, glared.**  

**“Then *why the fuck* do you let her keep it up?”**  

Bill, **eyebrows raising, voice suddenly sharper—**  

**“Oh, I don’t know, Jodi. Why the fuck are you demanding the *patriarchy* come to the *fucking rescue* of a woman exercising her *free will*?”**  

Jodi **froze.**  

Naomi, **mouth slightly open, glanced between them.**  

Bill, **leaning forward, expression pointed.**  

**“Doesn’t that fucking *not make any sense* to you?”**  

Jodi **felt her pulse spike.**  

Because—**shit.**  

He wasn’t **wrong.**  

But *fuck*, that didn’t make this **better.**

**“We just sit together. Maybe eat, maybe drink. Just *decompress*.”**

Jeff **stares at her**, **blinking once**.  

Bill **lets out a low whistle**. *“And there it is.”*

### **More Than a Legend**

**He’s being honest.**  

That’s Jeff. He never sugarcoats. He **doesn't hide from the truth**, even when it's ugly, even when it’s uncomfortable.  

But that last part?  

*"Rejection is the story of my life."*  

**That gets to her.**

*"That’s a little dramatic, don’t you think?"*

Jodi **leans forward**, eyes narrowing. *“And you’ve come back every time.”*

Because she lets him.

Because no matter what, no matter how long he’s gone, no matter how **many fuckups, or fuck-buddies, or fuckups with fuck-buddies**—
